### [175] [IA-RAG: Interval-Algebra-Driven Temporal Reasoning for Dynamic Knowledge Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06044)
*Xiaoman Wang,Yaoze Zhang,Wenzhuo Fan,Hongwei Zhang,Ding Wang,Guohang Yan,Song Mao,Botian Shi,Yunshi Lan,Pinlong Cai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: IA-RAG提出了一种分层时序RAG框架，将知识建模为时间区间（IEU），通过Allen区间代数进行时序约束检索，并引入子图时间收紧机制处理模糊时间边界，在多个时序QA基准上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG和Graph RAG框架将知识视为静态或仅关联粗粒度时间戳/元数据，无法捕获持续时间、重叠、包含等丰富的时序结构，限制了LLM在复杂时序推理任务上的表现。

Method: 1) 将事实表示为区间事件单元(IEU)并按层次组织为主题森林(Thematic Forest)；2) 使用Allen区间代数建模时序依赖关系；3) 提出子图时间收紧(Sub-graph Time Tightening)机制，通过事件子图内的逻辑约束细化模糊时间边界；4) 支持基于区间代数引导遍历的隐式时序语义检索。

Result: 在TimeQA、TempReason、ComplexTR等多个时序问答基准上，IA-RAG取得了强时序检索与推理性能，尤其在复杂组合时序推理任务上表现突出。

Conclusion: 通过引入区间级时序建模和严格的代数约束，IA-RAG有效提升了RAG系统对复杂时序知识的理解和推理能力，为细粒度时序知识检索提供了新范式。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has shown strong effectiveness in grounding Large Language Models (LLMs) with external knowledge. However, existing RAG and Graph RAG frameworks largely treat knowledge as static or associate time with coarse-grained timestamps or metadata, failing to capture rich temporal structures such as duration, overlap, and containment. We propose IA-RAG, a hierarchical temporal RAG framework that models knowledge as time intervals and performs retrieval under formal temporal constraints. IA-RAG represents facts as Interval Event Units (IEUs) and organizes them into a hierarchical Thematic Forest, where temporal dependencies are governed by Allen's Interval Algebra. To handle incomplete or uncertain temporal boundaries, IA-RAG further introduces a Sub-graph Time Tightening mechanism that refines fuzzy intervals through logical constraints within connected event subgraphs. In addition, IA-RAG supports implicit temporal semantic retrieval through interval-algebra-guided traversal. Experiments on multiple temporal question answering benchmarks, including TimeQA, TempReason, and ComplexTR, demonstrate that IA-RAG achieves strong temporal retrieval and reasoning performance, particularly on complex compositional temporal reasoning tasks. Our code is released at https://github.com/xiaoAugenstern/LogicalRAG_TemporalQA.

### [176] [Automatic Labelling of Speech Translation Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06047)

Abstract: Errors in speech translations reduce trustworthiness of Speech Translation (ST) systems and can have serious consequences. Yet currently there is no established methodology for evaluating confidence and quality estimation of speech translations. To initiate progress in this direction, we propose Speech Translation Error Labelling (STEL). We create an annotation protocol, a small authentic end-to-end evaluation dataset, and we analyse how existing text-only and speech-processing systems perform the STEL task. Our results show that text-only XCOMET and multimodal LLM Qwen2.5-Omni are able to perform the STEL task in roughly half the precision of humans. We also find that direct speech processing is necessary for the STEL task, and that the current text-only and speech-processing systems are complementary in labelling translation-only vs. speech-processing errors in ST.

### [177] [Multi-task Learning is Not Enough: Representational Entanglement in Dual-output Second Language Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06065)
*Seung Hwan Cho,Young-Min Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了多任务学习（MTL）在第二语言（L2）语音识别中的应用，发现MTL虽然能提升语义识别，但会降低表面转录（音素级）的准确性，尤其在英语中更为显著，且这种降解与表面-语义之间的编辑距离呈正相关。通过编码器和解码器分析，揭示了编码器层面的表征纠缠是导致该问题的关键原因，并提出了缓解纠缠的MTL框架设计方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多任务学习（MTL）认为共享表征对多个任务均有好处，但该假设在L2语音识别的双输出（表面转录和语义识别）场景下是否成立尚不清楚，本文旨在验证该假设并分析其失效原因。

Method: 采用多任务学习框架同时进行表面转录（音素级）和语义识别（意义级）任务；通过编码器分析考察任务表征的纠缠程度；通过跨任务解码器分析比较不同解码器对编码器输出的依赖模式。

Result: MTL提升语义识别但降低表面转录准确性，英语中降解程度与表面-语义间的Levenshtein编辑距离正相关；编码器分析显示韩语能保持分离的任务表征，而英语产生几乎一致的表征；解码器分析表明语义解码器能形成独特的表征，但表面解码器受限于编码器。

Conclusion: MTL在L2语音识别中面临编码器层面的表征纠缠问题，需要设计能够减轻编码器纠缠的MTL框架，以降低双输出L2自动语音识别中表面转录的性能退化。

Abstract: Second-language (L2) speech recognition often requires transcriptions of pronunciations and intended meanings. Multi-task learning (MTL) is a natural approach because it assumes that shared representations benefit both outputs. However, this paper shows that this assumption does not hold across Korean and English. MTL improves meaning but degrades surface transcription, especially in English, where the degradation scales with surface-meaning divergence measured by Levenshtein edit distance.Encoder analysis links these patterns to encoder-level entanglement, with Korean preserving distinct task representations while English produces nearly identical ones. Cross-task decoder analysis shows that the meaning dual-output decoder adapts with a unique representation, while the surface dual-output decoder remains constrained by the encoder. These findings motivate the design of MTL frameworks that mitigate encoder-level entanglement to reduce surface degradation in dual-output L2 automatic speech recognition.

</details>


### [178] [SkillComposer: Learning to Evolve Agent Skills for Specification and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06079)
*Qi Zhang,Zhaopeng Feng,Xiaonan Shi,Xiaomeng Hu,Chu Liu,Pengjun Xie,Xiaobin Wang,Jieping Ye,Bryan Hooi,Haobo Wang,Junbo Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SkillComposer提出了一种将技能构建分解为创建、改进和合并三种可学习操作的框架，通过拒绝采样训练使语言模型在推理时自我进化技能，在多项基准测试中显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前技能构建方法采用一次性提取方式，面临根本性矛盾：针对特定任务的技能难以迁移，而抽象化的技能又缺乏足够指导。这种脆弱性源于缺乏技能特化与泛化的显式机制。

Method: SkillComposer将技能构建分解为三个可学习操作（创建、改进、合并），通过系统性拒绝采样策略训练，使语言模型在推理时实现技能自我进化。支持离线（构建通用库）、在线（任务特化）和混合三种部署模式。

Conclusion: 合并和改进操作解决了正交的质量维度问题，技能组合是一种可迁移的元能力，为技能增强型推理提供了实用方案。

Abstract: Agent skills, which consist of reusable strategies that guide agent reasoning and action, have shown strong potential for improving model capability at inference time. However, current skill construction methods treat the problem as one-shot extraction, overlooking a fundamental tension: a skill tailored to the specific task fails to transfer, while the abstracted skill often provides insufficient guidance. We attribute this fragility to the absence of explicit mechanisms for skill specification and generalization. To address this gap, we introduce SkillComposer, a framework that decomposes skill construction into three learnable operations: create, improve, and merge. Trained via systematic rejection sampling recipe, SkillComposer enables language models to self-evolve skills at inference time and supports three deployment modes: offline for building generalized libraries, online for task-specific refinement, and hybrid for combining both. Comprehensive experiments on $τ^2$-Bench, LiveCodeBench v6, and AppWorld show that SkillComposer consistently outperforms baselines. Our SkillComposer-4B improves a 27B executor by up to +4.5 on agent tasks and +3.4 on code tasks, while generalizing across domains and task types unseen during training. Analysis reveals that merge and improve address orthogonal quality dimensions and that skill composition is a transferable meta-ability, providing a practical recipe for skill-augmented inference.

### [179] [LatentSkill: From In-Context Textual Skills to In-Weight Latent Skills for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06087)
*Aofan Yu,Chenyu Zhou,Tianyi Xu,Zihan Guo,Rong Shan,Zhihui Fu,Jun Wang,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang,Jianghao Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LatentSkill将文本技能转换为可插拔的LoRA适配器，将技能知识存储在权重空间而非上下文空间，在ALFWorld和Search-QA上显著减少了预填充token数量，同时提升了任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统智能体系统在每一步都将文本技能注入提示词中，导致大量上下文开销，并且技能内容以明文形式暴露，存在安全隐患。

Method: 通过预训练的超网络将文本技能转换为即插即用的LoRA适配器，技能知识存储在权重空间，支持模块化加载、缩放和组合。

Result: 在ALFWorld上，seen和unseen分片成功率分别提升21.4和13.4个百分点，预填充token减少64.1%；在Search-QA上，精确匹配提升3.0个百分点，技能token开销降低72.2%。

Conclusion: 权重空间技能为扩展LLM智能体提供了一种高效、模块化且暴露度更低的方案，生成的技能LoRA具有结构化的语义几何，可通过LoRA缩放系数精确控制，并支持参数空间算术组合。

Abstract: Agent systems increasingly use textual skills to encode reusable task procedures, but injecting these skills into the prompt at every step incurs substantial context overhead and exposes skill content as plaintext. We present LatentSkill, a framework that converts textual skills into plug-and-play LoRA adapters through a pretrained hypernetwork. LatentSkill stores skill knowledge in weight space rather than context space, removing per-step skill tokens while preserving modular loading, scaling, and composition. On ALFWorld and Search-QA, LatentSkill outperforms the corresponding in-context skill baseline while using substantially fewer prefill tokens: it improves ALFWorld success by 21.4 and 13.4 points on the seen and unseen splits with 64.1% fewer prefill tokens, and improves Search-QA exact match by 3.0 points with 72.2% lower skill-token overhead. Further analysis shows that generated skill LoRAs form a structured semantic geometry, can be precisely controlled via the LoRA scaling coefficient, and can be composed through parameter-space arithmetic when skill components are aligned. These findings suggest that weight-space skills provide an efficient, modular, and less exposed substrate for extending LLM agents.

Abstract: We present CHALIS (Challenging Language Identification Samples), a new benchmark dataset explicitly designed to address difficult cases in language identification: cousin languages and orthographic noise. Our dataset has two parts: First, we collected sentences shared across mutually intelligible language pairs (Czech/Slovak, Spanish/Catalan, Portuguese/Galician, Danish/Norwegian). The second part tests for orthography noise: we transliterate text across multiple scripts, remove diacritics, simulate homoglyph attacks, and use Internet slang. We evaluate four widely used language identification systems on CHALIS and demonstrate that all struggle substantially in these scenarios, especially on lower-resource languages within cousin pairs and on transliterated input. Abstract: Entity alignment (EA) aims to identify equivalent entities across heterogeneous knowledge graphs (KGs) and is a key component of knowledge fusion and cross-KG reasoning. The recent EA foundation model demonstrates that alignment knowledge, once pretrained, can be directly applied to diverse previously unseen KG pairs. However, it still underuses structural context in two places: cross-KG interaction is weak during encoding, and final candidate ranking still relies too heavily on coarse similarity. We address these limitations with ContextEA, an enhanced encoder-decoder framework for transferable EA. On the encoder side, we introduce a cross-KG interaction encoder that unifies the two KGs with anchor bridges and performs earlier relation-aware cross-graph propagation. On the decoder side, we introduce a structural calibration decoder that calibrates alignment scores with entity-level, neighborhood-level, relation-level, and anchor-aware structural evidence. This design strengthens both structural context construction and structural context exploitation while remaining lightweight. Experiments on 29 EA datasets in OpenEA, SRPRS, and DBP show consistent gains over strong transferable baselines. These results suggest that explicitly harnessing structural context is an effective direction for improving EA foundation models.

Moreover, among quality metrics, we find that QA-based evaluation is a substantially stronger predictor of real-world usability than standard approaches.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent work has sought to understand Large Language Models (LLMs) reasoning, yet a principled, model-intrinsic signal that captures its layer-wise reasoning dynamics remains underexplored. Using Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) as a diagnostic probe, we observe that LLMs' internal reasoning is marked by a sharp increase in reasoning feature activations concentrated in late layers. Motivated by this pattern, we establish a formal link between reasoning intensity and the model's latent geometry and theoretically prove that the l2 norm of hidden states bounds the activation strength of SAE reasoning features. Empirical correlation analysis and causal interventions further validate the l2 norm as a faithful indicator, where heightened norms consistently correspond to critical reasoning steps.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Input length and the position of relevant information are widely cited as the primary causes of degraded LLM long-context performance. Here, we study lexical density -- the rate at which a context introduces distinct information -- as a third, largely overlooked factor that systematically reduces the effective context window of LLMs. We quantify the impact of lexical density on open-weight LLMs (9B-685B) using three "find-the-needle" style benchmarks with identical length (~12k tokens) and controlled needle position, but increasing density of information. We observe a sharp performance collapse in higher-density benchmarks: models that are near-perfect in sparse contexts drop below 60% retrieval score on denser ones. To rule out task-type confounds, we vary and control the density within each benchmark while keeping all other properties unchanged. Reducing density generally restores performance, especially in the high-density regimes where degradation appears. These results show that effective context capacity is a function of lexical density, with direct implications for real-world LLM systems operating on compact, information-rich inputs.

Motivation: 标准ASR在病理语音上的表现不佳，需要有效的说话人自适应方法，同时避免对预训练模型权重的大规模修改。

Method: 使用FiLM（Feature-wise Linear Modulation）将x-vector说话人嵌入注入冻结ASR编码器的每一层Transformer中，实现对病理说话人的自适应；与标准微调和参数高效微调基线对比，并辅以后处理。

Result: 说话人条件化ASR在病理语音上与已有自适应策略竞争力相当，且能保持对非条件化语音的性能，同时保留语音相关问题回答能力。

Conclusion: FiLM-based说话人条件化是一种有效的病理语音自适应方法，兼具性能与模型可迁移性。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition (ASR) has advanced remarkably for standard speech; however, pathological speech from neurological conditions remains a significant challenge. We investigate speaker conditioning via Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM), injecting x-vector-derived information into each transformer layer of a frozen ASR encoder to adapt internal representations to individual pathological speakers without modifying base model weights. We benchmark this for the ASR task against standard and parameter-efficient fine-tuning baselines, complemented by post-processing, on Spanish and English pathological speech. Additionally, we evaluate if the adapted model preserves the ability to answer speech-related questions. Results show that speaker-conditioned ASR is competitive with established adaptation strategies while retaining performance on non-conditioned speech.

In this work, we introduce a benchmark dataset and evaluation framework for \textit{data snapshot extraction}, the task of identifying and localizing semantically meaningful visual artifacts within institutional documents. The benchmark spans humanitarian reports, World Bank policy research working papers, and project appraisal documents, and includes annotations for figures and tables that contain reusable analytical information. Using this dataset, we benchmarked multiple open-source layout detection models and evaluated both detection performance and spatial extraction quality. Our results show that current models struggle to generalize to operational institutional documents despite strong performance on conventional academic benchmarks. Common failure modes include confusion between analytical and non-analytical content, fragmentation of composite analytical artifacts, and incomplete extraction of contextual information required for interpretation. These findings highlight a persistent gap between generic document layout analysis and operationally useful data snapshot extraction. We release the source PDFs, annotation dataset, metadata, and source code to support future research in operational document intelligence. ### [189] [From Self to Other: Evaluating Demographic Perspective-Taking in LLM Hate Speech Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06266)
*Paloma Piot,Javier Parapar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文评估了人物条件化大语言模型在模拟不同人口群体对仇恨言论感知分歧方面的能力，发现没有模型能一致地捕捉人类判断的所有三个维度（群体间分歧、内群体敏感性、替代性预测），但使用Llama 3.1的替代性提示在多数人口维度上最接近人类分歧模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仇恨言论检测本质上具有主观性，不同人口群体对同一内容的感知差异显著。收集来自多个群体的标注数据成本高昂且难以规模化，因此研究者提出使用人物条件化大语言模型（通过提示词让模型采用特定人口身份）来大规模模拟多样化视角，但需要验证这些模型是否真正反映了不同群体间的分歧方式。

Method: 评估了人物条件化LLM在三个方面的人类社会判断能力：(i)不同群体人物是否以类似人类的方式产生分歧（群体间分歧），(ii)当内容针对自身身份时是否变得更敏感（内群体敏感性），(iii)是否能准确预测其他群体的反应（替代性预测）。比较了不同模型和提示配置的表现。

Result: 没有模型能一致地捕捉所有三个维度，性能高度依赖于具体模型，并不能仅通过最小的身份提示词可靠地涌现。但Llama 3.1的替代性提示在大多数人口维度上取得了最高的跨群体一致性，并提供了最接近人类分歧模式的整体近似。

Conclusion: 当前的人物条件化模型在模拟人类群体分歧方面仍存在局限，不能简单地依赖最小身份提示。但Llama 3.1结合替代性提示可能为自动标注提供更可靠的设置，使其更接近人类判断。

Abstract: Hate speech detection is inherently subjective: people from different demographic groups perceive the same content very differently. Collecting enough annotations from multiple demographic groups is costly and difficult to scale. Persona-conditioned Large Language Models (models prompted to adopt a specific demographic identity) have been proposed as a way to simulate diverse perspectives at scale. But do they actually reflect how different groups disagree? We evaluate three aspects of human social judgement: (i) whether personas from different groups disagree in human-like ways (inter-group disagreement), (ii) whether they become more sensitive when content targets their own identity (in-group sensitivity), and (iii) whether they can accurately predict how another group would react (vicarious prediction). Our results show that no model consistently captures all three dimensions, and performance is highly model-dependent and does not emerge reliably from minimal identity prompts alone. However, vicarious prompting with Llama 3.1 yields the highest cross-group agreement in most demographic axes and provides the closest overall approximation to human disagreement patterns, indicating that this configuration may provide a more reliable setting for automatic annotation aligned with human judgements.

### [190] [Many Circuits, One Mechanism: Input Variation and Evaluation Granularity in Circuit Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06267)
*Alireza Bayat Makou,Jingcheng Niu,Subhabrata Dutta,Iryna Gurevych*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现电路结构差异不一定反映功能差异，提出了“幻影特化”现象：不同频带上的电路结构不同但功能相同，标准评估方法会掩盖这一事实，需使用边级评估和跨条件迁移测试才能揭示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验电路发现中一个常见但未经严格验证的假设——电路结构差异等同于机制差异。

Method: 在固定任务（文字序列复制）下改变输入统计特征（四种词频带+对照条件），在五个Pythia模型（70M-1.4B）中提取75个电路，使用边级评估和跨条件迁移测试分析结构与功能的关系。

Result: 结构不同的电路实现相同计算：频带特异边可跨频带迁移，核心共享边恢复至少99%性能，因果干预证实表征可互换；同一频带内多次提取表明发现算法采样的是等价类而非唯一机制；源级评估夸大忠实度，边级评估揭示结构到功能的多对一映射。

Conclusion: 电路结构差异不足以证明机制差异，必须使用边级评估和跨条件迁移测试来验证功能等价性。

Abstract: Circuit discovery methods identify subgraphs that explain specific model behaviors, and structural differences between discovered circuits are commonly interpreted as evidence of distinct mechanisms. We test this assumption by varying input statistics while holding the task fixed, and show that the resulting structural differences exhibit apparent specialization but do not correspond to functional differences, a pattern we term phantom specialization. Using Literal Sequence Copying across four token-frequency bands plus a control condition in five Pythia models (70M-1.4B), we extract 75 circuits and find that structurally distinct circuits implement the same computation: band-specific edges transfer broadly across bands, a core shared across most bands recovers at least 99% of circuit performance, and causal interchange interventions confirm that internal representations are interchangeable across frequency bands. Repeated extractions within the same frequency band further suggest that discovery algorithms sample from an equivalence class of valid subgraphs rather than recovering a unique mechanism. Standard evaluation practice obscures this pattern: source-level evaluation inflates apparent faithfulness, while edge-level evaluation reveals the many-to-one mapping from structure to function. Our results show that structural differences between circuits are not sufficient evidence for distinct mechanisms, and that exposing this requires edge-level evaluation and cross-condition transfer tests.

### [191] [FOXGLOVE: Understanding Goal-Oriented and Anchored Writing Feedback from Experts and LLMs on Argumentative Essays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06271)
*Yijun Liu,Yifan Song,John Gallagher,Sarah Sterman,Tal August*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型越来越多地被用于生成写作反馈，但目前缺乏在写作研究认为对修改至关重要的维度上（目标导向、句子锚定、优先级排序）对LLM和专家反馈进行系统比较的研究。

Method: 构建FOXGLOVE数据集，包含69篇12年级议论文的696条训练有素的写作教师反馈，以及4个前沿LLM在共享协议下生成的1,644条评论，总计2,340条评论。对教师和LLM评论的子集提供专家质量评分。

Conclusion: FOXGLOVE数据集使得系统比较人类与LLM反馈在哪些方面一致、分歧和存在差异成为可能。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate writing feedback, there remains no systematic comparison of LLM and expert feedback on the dimensions that writing research identifies as central to revision: goal-orientation, anchoring to specific sentences, and prioritization. We introduce FOXGLOVE, a dataset of 696 feedback comments written by trained writing instructors on 69 twelfth-grade argumentative essays, paired with 1,644 comments generated from four frontier LLMs under a shared protocol, totaling 2,340 comments. We provide expert quality ratings on a subset of both instructor and LLM comments. We find that instructors and LLMs distribute feedback similarly across goals and essay positions, yet instructors and models diverge on the specific sentences on which to provide feedback. Additionally, we find that models tend to write more complex feedback and use fewer questions than instructors. LLM feedback also receives higher ratings on most dimensions of quality, as rated by instructors, but much of this advantage appears to be attributable to lengthier comments. FOXGLOVE enables systematic comparison of where human and LLM feedback align, diverge, and differ.

### [192] [LLMs Can Leak Training Data But Do They Want To? A Propensity-Aware Evaluation of Memorization in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06286)
*Gianluca Barmina,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出PropMe框架，用于区分大语言模型在对抗性攻击下的记忆提取能力（capability）与正常使用中的实际泄露倾向（propensity），并引入SimpleTrace工具进行轻量级溯源评估。实验表明，模型在对抗性提示下能泄露训练数据，但在非对抗环境中泄露率很低，且持续预训练可降低记忆倾向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆化评估大多测量模型在被迫（如前缀攻击）下能否复现训练数据，而非测量其在普通使用中是否真的复现，因此缺乏对实际泄露风险的认知。

Method: 提出PropMe框架，包含(a) 基于度量变换将能力指标转换为倾向指标；(b) SimpleTrace轻量溯源管线，基于infini-gram将生成结果确定性归因至大规模训练语料；(c) 对比前缀攻击（能力评估）与非对抗性提示（倾向评估）下的逐字、近逐字及倾向转换记忆指标。

Result: 在Comma和DFM Decoder两个模型、Common Pile和Dynaword两个数据集上，前缀攻击引发的记忆信号远强于通用提示或数据集特定提示，而倾向分数整体较低。DFM Decoder（从Comma持续预训练而来）在Common Pile上的记忆能力和倾向均降低。

Conclusion: 记忆审计应同时报告最坏情况下的可提取性（capability）和日常使用中的泄露倾向（propensity），以获得更全面的记忆化视图。

Abstract: Large language models can reproduce training data, but existing memorization evaluations mostly measure whether models can be forced to do so, rather than whether they do so under ordinary use. We introduce PropMe, a propensity-aware framework for memorization evaluation that contrasts prefix-based capability attacks with non-adversarial evaluations. We propose a metric transformation that, applied to existing functions, allows to create propensity metrics. We further introduce SimpleTrace, a lightweight tracing pipeline built on infini-gram that deterministically attributes model generations to large-scale training corpora and computes verbatim, near-verbatim, and propensity-transformed memorization metrics. Evaluating two fully-open models: Comma and DFM Decoder on two datasets: Common Pile and Dynaword in two languages, we find a consistent gap between capability and propensity: prefix attacks elicit substantially stronger memorization signals than generic or dataset-specific prompts, while propensity scores remain low overall. Thus, the models can reveal training data when directly elicited, but rarely do so in more common non-adversarial settings. We also find that DFM Decoder, which is continually pre-trained from Comma, exhibits reduced memorization and memorization propensity for Common Pile, confirming that memorization capability can decrease when later training emphasizes partially different data. Our results suggest, and we encourage, that memorization audits should report both worst-case extractability and ordinary leakage propensity in order to have a more comprehensive view of this phenomenon.

</details>


### [193] [Decomposing Factual Sycophancy in Language Models: How Size and Instruction Tuning Shape Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06306)
*Victor De Marez,Luna De Bruyne,Walter Daelemans*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文分解了事实性从众（factual sycophancy）为两个机制：真理边际（truth margin）和操纵敏感性（manipulation sensitivity），并通过对56个开源模型（0.3B-32B参数）和13种操纵类型的分析，发现模型脆弱性主要由规模决定，但指令微调会改变规模的作用方式：小模型经指令微调后鲁棒性下降，大模型则提升。指令微调主要增加真理边际，但行为效果取决于操纵类型。缩放对两个通道的影响也不同：基座模型边际增加但操纵敏感性轻微上升，指令微调模型边际增长更快且敏感性下降。因此，事实性从众不是单一标量属性，评估应报告通道特定、操纵特定和规模条件下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将事实性从众简化为单一翻转率指标，但翻转率混淆了模型对真理的基线偏好强度（真理边际）和被社会压力偏移的程度（操纵敏感性）这两个不同机制。作者希望将这两个通道解耦，以更精细地理解模型规模、指令微调对鲁棒性的不同影响机制。

Method: 对56个开源模型（0.3B-32B参数）进行13种操纵类型的实验，将翻转率分解为真理边际（模型对正确答案的基线偏好）和操纵敏感性（社会压力偏移真理边际的程度），并分别分析模型规模和指令微调对这两个通道的影响。

Result: 1）模型脆弱性主要由规模决定；2）指令微调改变规模的作用方式：小模型经指令微调后鲁棒性下降，大模型则提升；3）指令微调主要增加真理边际，但行为效果取决于操纵类型；4）缩放对两个通道影响不同：基座模型边际增加但敏感性轻微上升，指令微调模型边际增长更快且敏感性下降。

Conclusion: 事实性从众不是单一标量属性，评估应报告通道特定、操纵特定和规模条件下的鲁棒性，而非仅报告翻转率。

Abstract: Factual sycophancy occurs when a language model abandons a correct, verifiable answer under social pressure. Because a flip occurs only when pressure toward a false answer exceeds the model's neutral preference for the truth, flip rates conflate two mechanisms: the strength of that baseline preference (truth margin), and how far pressure shifts it (manipulation sensitivity). We decompose factual sycophancy into these channels and use them to separate the effects of size and instruction tuning across 56 open-weight models spanning 0.3B-32B parameters and 13 manipulation types. We find that vulnerability is governed mainly by size, but instruction tuning changes how size acts: small instruction-tuned models can become less robust, whereas large instruction-tuned models usually become more robust. Instruction tuning primarily increases truth margin, but its behavioral effect depends on manipulation type. Scaling also changes the two channels differently: base models gain margin but become mildly more manipulation-sensitive, whereas instruction-tuned models gain margin faster and become less sensitive. Factual sycophancy is therefore not a single scalar property. Evaluations should report channel-specific, manipulation-specific, and size-conditioned robustness rather than flip rates alone.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对伦巴第语的平行语料和单语语料进行人工审计，分析网络爬取数据集、精选语料库和基准测试中有效伦巴第语部分的正字法构成，评估语言识别错误、样板文本和噪声污染程度。

Result: 网络爬取的大规模数据集存在严重的语言识别错误、样板文本和非语言噪声；高质量语料严重偏向西部伦巴第方言变体，东部方言被边缘化；各语料库之间存在相互冲突的正字法系统。

Conclusion: 需要开展面向方言变体、由社区驱动的数据策展工作，而非纯粹追求数量的数据爬取。

Abstract: Several of the world's languages are still under-resourced in terms of Natural Language Processing (NLP) tools. This is mostly due to the lack of high-quality datasets to train, develop, and evaluate systems and models for several tasks, such as Machine Translation (MT). We conduct a manual audit of the parallel and monolingual corpora available for Lombard, an under-resourced language continuum from Italy. Our analysis reveals that the perceived abundance of web-scraped data is an illusion, with massive datasets plagued by severe language misidentification, boilerplate text, and non-linguistic noise. Furthermore, we analyze the orthographic composition of the valid Lombard portions across web-scraped datasets, curated corpora, and benchmarks. Our findings show conflicting orthographical systems and severe representational bias across all corpora: high-quality data is heavily skewed towards Western Lombard varieties, with Eastern ones left on the margins. This underscores the need for variety-aware, community-driven data curation rather than purely quantity-driven scraping.

### [195] [EDIT: Evidence-Diagnosed Intervention Training for Rule-Faithful LLM Grading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06350)
*Zhihao Wu,Linhai Zhang,Taiyi Wang,Runcong Zhao,Peter Andrews,Cesare Aloisi,Yulan He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评分模型仅追求分数预测准确率，但缺乏对评分推理过程是否忠实于评分标准和学生答案的验证；现有的归因和干预方法主要针对数学等自包含推理任务，无法有效识别评分推理中的错误步骤或模型对最终分数的信念变化。

Method: EDIT包含两个阶段：(1) EDIT-SFT利用内部模型信号（最终分数的后验信念和输入归因分数）定位问题推理步骤，并借助评分清单进行局部修正；(2) EDIT-RL采用信念引导的奖励塑形，惩罚有害的信念漂移同时允许有益的探索。

Result: 在两个真实多学科评分基准上，EDIT在域内和域外分割上均持续优于强SFT和RL基线，消融实验证实内部状态诊断是性能提升的关键驱动因素。

Conclusion: 通过结合内部模型信号进行局部推理修正和信念引导的奖励塑形，能有效提升LLM评分器对评分标准的忠实度，且该方法具有良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: Reliable rubric grading requires more than accurate score prediction. Each judgement must be grounded in the mark scheme and evidence from the student answer. Existing credit-assignment and intervention methods, primarily designed for self-contained reasoning tasks such as mathematics reasoning, struggle in this setting because they do not identify where grading reasoning goes wrong or how the model's belief about the final mark changes during reasoning. We propose Evidence-Diagnosed Intervention Training (EDIT), a two-phase framework for training more rubric-faithful LLM graders. First, EDIT-SFT locates problematic reasoning steps using internal model signals: posterior belief over the final mark and input-grounding scores. It then revises only these local steps with help from a rubric checklist. Second, EDIT-RL calibrates the grader with belief-guided reward shaping, penalising large harmful belief drifts while still allowing helpful exploration. Experiments on two real-world, multi-subject grading benchmarks demonstrate that EDIT consistently outperforms strong supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning baselines on both in-domain and out-of-domain splits, with ablation studies confirming that internal-state diagnostics drive these gains.

</details>

Abstract: The question of whether artificial systems can be conscious remains open, in part because existing approaches either evaluate systems against theory-derived checklists (discriminative) or engineer consciousness-inspired modules directly (architectural); both leave open whether observed structures are artifacts of human language priors. We propose a generative methodology: emergent language (EL) in multi-agent reinforcement learning, where agents start from minimal (no language, no concept of self, minimal exposure to human text) and develop communication under task pressure alone, ensuring causal attributability to task demands rather than inherited human language priors. We position our methodology by discussing how EL serves as a generative tool for studying consciousness-relevant structure, including the role of environment complexity and the interpretation of emergent communication. As a proof of concept, we instantiate this methodology in a minimal environment and show that agents develop self-referential communication, including an echo-mismatch detection circuit that is not predicted by task structure or architecture alone but emerges from a specific environmental affordance.

To enable a systematic analysis of agents' collaborative competence in MAS, we introduce CollabSim, a configurable simulation framework that combines a theory-grounded definition of collaborative capabilities, controlled manipulation of interaction conditions, and action-level probing of agents' internal states. We use this setup to compare modern large language models on Komi-Yazva-to-Russian translation under severe parallel-data scarcity in zero-shot and retrieval-based few-shot regimes. ### [201] [Latent Reasoning with Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06447)
*Guancheng Tu,Xiangjun Fu,Suhao Yu,Yao Tang,Haoqiang Kang,Lianhui Qin,Yizhe Zhang,Jiatao Gu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: NF-CoT通过归一化流在大型语言模型中实现连续潜在推理，既保留了显式思维链的关键优势（如自左向右生成、概率采样、KV缓存兼容性），又通过紧凑连续状态降低了推理成本，在代码生成任务上提升了通过率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 显式思维链（CoT）将中间计算强制为离散、串行、面向通信的token流，每个推理步骤必须被语言化后才能继续，即使底层更新是语义化、不确定或仅部分成形的。现有潜在推理方法牺牲了CoT在自回归语言模型中的关键优势。

Method: 在LLM骨干网络内实例化TARFlow风格的归一化流，为从显式CoT蒸馏出的紧凑连续思维定义可处理的概率模型。连续思维位置由NF头生成，文本位置由标准LM头在同一因果流中生成，支持精确似然估计、概率性左到右解码和潜在推理空间的直接策略梯度优化。

Result: 在代码生成基准上，NF-CoT相比显式CoT和先前潜在推理基线提高了通过率，同时显著降低了中间推理成本。

Abstract: Large language models often improve reasoning by generating explicit chain-of-thought (CoT), demonstrating the importance of intermediate computation. However, textual CoT forces this computation through a discrete, serial, and communication-oriented token stream: each reasoning step must be verbalized before the model can proceed, even when the underlying update is semantic, uncertain, or only partially formed. Latent reasoning offers a higher-bandwidth alternative by performing intermediate computation in compact continuous states before committing to text. Yet existing latent-reasoning methods often sacrifice key advantages that make CoT effective in autoregressive language models, including native left-to-right generation, probabilistic sampling, compatibility with KV-cache decoding, and tractable likelihood estimation. We propose NF-CoT, a latent reasoning framework that preserves these advantages by modeling continuous thoughts with normalizing flows. NF-CoT instantiates a TARFlow-style normalizing flow inside the LLM backbone, defining a tractable probability model over compact continuous thoughts distilled from explicit CoT. Continuous-thought positions are generated by an NF head, while text positions are generated by the standard LM head within the same causal stream. This design provides exact likelihoods for latent thoughts, enables probabilistic left-to-right decoding with the original KV cache, and supports direct policy-gradient optimization in the latent reasoning space. On code-generation benchmarks, NF-CoT improves pass rates over explicit-CoT and prior latent-reasoning baselines while substantially reducing intermediate-reasoning cost.

### [202] [Human Adults and LLMs as Scientists: Who Benefits from Active Exploration?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06464)
*Mandana Samiei,Eunice Yiu,Anthony GX-Chen,Dongyan Lin,Jocelyn Shen,Blake A. Richards,Alison Gopnik,Doina Precup*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了主动探索是否能改善成年人在合取因果规则学习中的表现，发现主动探索显著提升了合取因果推理能力，但合取规则仍需更多测试；与大型语言模型相比，部分模型在假设推断准确性上接近人类水平，但探索效率较低且存在类似的合取-析取差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究表明成年人在识别合取因果规则（多个原因同时存在才能导致结果）时存在困难，即"合取障碍"，但多数研究采用被动观察范式，学习者无法控制证据生成。本文想探究当赋予成年人主动探索权时，这种偏见是否依然存在。

Method: 使用改进的"blicket detector"任务，让成年参与者在合取或析取规则结构下自由干预以识别因果对象，同时将人类表现与多种大型语言模型在同一设置下进行比较。

Result: 主动探索显著改善了成年人的合取因果推理，但合取规则仍需比析取规则更多的测试才能推断出来。部分大语言模型在假设推断准确性上接近人类水平，但探索策略效率较低，且表现出类似的合取-析取性能差距。

Conclusion: 主动探索能够有效缓解但无法完全消除合取因果推理中的困难；当前最先进的大语言模型在因果推理准确性上接近人类，但在探索效率和策略上仍有差距。

Abstract: A long-standing finding in the causal learning literature is that adults struggle to identify conjunctive causal rules, where an effect requires the simultaneous presence of multiple causes, while performing better in disjunctive settings. However, most demonstrations of this ``conjunctive handicap'' rely on passive observation paradigms with limited evidence, where learners have no control over evidence generation. This paper asks whether this bias persists when adults are granted agency through active exploration. Using a modified ``blicket detector'' task, adult participants freely intervened to identify causal objects under conjunctive or disjunctive rule structures. We show that active exploration substantially improves adults' conjunctive causal reasoning, although conjunctive rules still require more tests to infer than disjunctive rules. We further compare human performance to a range of large language models in the same setting. While some state-of-the-art models approach human-level performance on hypothesis inference accuracy, they often exhibit less efficient exploration strategies and similar conjunctive-disjunctive performance gaps.

### [203] [You Only Index Once: Cross-Layer Sparse Attention with Shared Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06467)
*Yutao Sun,Yanqi Zhang,Li Dong,Jianyong Wang,Furu Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出跨层稀疏注意力(CLSA)，基于KV共享架构(YOCO)，通过跨层共享KV缓存和路由索引，在保持token级细粒度选择性的同时分摊路由开销，实现了7.6倍解码加速和17.1倍整体吞吐提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文推理中，现有稀疏注意力方法存在效率与质量的权衡：结构化块稀疏方法加速强但质量损失大，token稀疏方法精度高但因全缓存top-k路由开销大而导致端到端加速有限。

Method: 在KV共享架构(YOCO)基础上，不仅跨解码器层共享KV缓存，还共享路由索引。由单个索引器计算token级top-k选择，结果在各层复用，既保留token稀疏注意力的细粒度选择性，又分摊了路由计算开销。

Result: 在短上下文和长上下文基准测试中，CLSA在128K上下文长度下实现高达7.6倍解码加速和17.1倍整体吞吐提升，同时保持模型质量。

Conclusion: CLSA提供了一种更完整的架构解决方案，能联合推进长上下文LLM的模型质量与推理效率，同时改善预填充、KV缓存存储和长上下文解码等所有主要推理瓶颈。

Abstract: Long-context inference in modern LLMs is increasingly constrained by decoding efficiency, especially in reasoning-heavy settings where models generate long intermediate chains of thought. Existing sparse attention methods often face a practical efficiency-quality trade-off. Structured block sparse methods typically provide stronger acceleration but incur noticeable quality loss, while token sparse methods are usually more accurate yet deliver limited end-to-end speedup because top-k routing over the full cache remains expensive. In this work, we propose cross-layer sparse attention (CLSA), which is built on top of KV-sharing architectures such as YOCO. The core idea is to share not only the KV cache across cross-decoder layers, but also the routing index. A single indexer computes token-level top-k selection once and reuses the resulting index across layers, thereby preserving the fine-grained selectivity of token sparse attention while amortizing the routing overhead. The resulting architecture improves all major inference bottlenecks jointly, including pre-filling, KV-cache storage, and long-context decoding. Experiments across short-context and long-context benchmarks show that CLSA is both accurate and efficient, achieving up to 7.6x decoding speedup and 17.1x overall throughput improvement at 128K context. These results suggest a more complete architectural solution for long-context LLMs that jointly advances model quality and inference efficiency.

</details>


### [204] [Self-Augmenting Retrieval for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06474)
*Paul Jünger,Justin Lovelace,Linxi Zhao,Dongyoung Go,Kilian Q. Weinberger*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SARDI框架，利用离散扩散语言模型在去噪过程中丢弃的低置信度token作为前瞻信号，动态指导检索增强生成，在无需训练的情况下显著提升多跳问答任务的效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散语言模型在去噪过程中会丢弃低置信度token，但这些被丢弃的token往往包含有用信息（如实体名称），可以提前指导检索以获取更强证据；而现有方法未能利用这一信号。

Method: 提出SARDI框架，在扩散模型的去噪轨迹中，利用每一步被丢弃的低置信度token作为"前瞻"信号来触发检索，将检索到的证据注入后续去噪步骤，无需额外训练且与检索器无关。

Result: 在5个多跳问答基准上，SARDI优于当前无需训练的扩散和自回归检索基线，同时吞吐量提升高达8倍。

Conclusion: 被丢弃的token包含有价值的实体信息，可作为检索信号；SARDI框架训练无关、与检索器无关、适用于任意可推理的离散扩散模型，展示了扩散模型在RAG任务中的独特优势。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion language models generate text by iteratively denoising an entire response in parallel. At each step, they predict tentative tokens for every masked position, committing the confident predictions to the output and discarding the unconfident ones. We show that the discarded tokens are in fact a useful lookahead signal for retrieval-augmented generation: even low-confidence tokens often surface salient entities early in the denoising trajectory, enabling retrieval of stronger evidence before the output is finalized. We exploit this through Self-Augmenting Retrieval for Diffusion Language Models (SARDI), a dynamic RAG framework that uses these lookahead tokens to guide retrieval during denoising. SARDI is training-free, retriever-agnostic, and applicable to any reasoning-capable discrete diffusion language model. Across five multi-hop QA benchmarks, SARDI outperforms current training-free diffusion and autoregressive retrieval baselines at up to $8\times$ higher throughput.

### [205] [Operation-Guided Progressive Human-to-AI Text Transformation Benchmark for Multi-Granularity AI-Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06481)
*Sondos Mahmoud Bsharat,Jiacheng Liu,Xiaohan Zhao,Tianjun Yao,Xinyi Shang,Yi Tang,Jiacheng Cui,Ahmed Elhagry,Salwa K. Al Khatib,Hao Li,Salman Khan,Zhiqiang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: OpAI-Bench是一个面向渐进式人机共同编辑场景的基准测试，通过9个渐进修订版本和5种AI编辑操作，系统研究AI文本可检测性在文档、句子、token和跨度粒度上的演化规律，发现可检测性不仅受AI编辑比例影响，还受编辑操作、领域和累积修订历史影响，并且混合作者身份的中间版本比纯人工或高度AI编辑版本更难检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI文本检测基准主要关注最终输出，无法理解AI作者身份信号在渐进式人机共同编辑过程中如何出现、累积或消失。

Method: 从人工撰写文档出发，对每个样本在预定义AI覆盖水平和5种代表性AI编辑操作下构建9个渐进修订版本，覆盖4个领域，并在多粒度（文档、句子、token、跨度）上保留完整作者身份溯源。

Result: AI文本可检测性受AI编辑比例、编辑操作类型、领域和累积修订历史共同影响；混合作者身份的中间版本比纯人工或高度AI编辑端点更难检测，呈现非单调检测模式。

Conclusion: OpAI-Bench为分析AI辅助写作在真实渐进编辑场景下何时以及如何变得可检测提供了受控测试平台。

Abstract: As AI writing assistants become increasingly integrated into real-world drafting and revision workflows, many documents are no longer purely human-written or AI-generated, but instead result from progressive human-AI co-editing. However, existing AI-text detection benchmarks largely focus on final outputs and provide limited understanding of how AI authorship signals emerge, accumulate, or disappear throughout the revision process. We introduce OpAI-Bench, an operation-guided benchmark for studying progressive human-to-AI text transformation across document, sentence, token, and span granularities. Starting from human-written documents, OpAI-Bench constructs nine sequentially revised versions for each sample under predefined AI coverage levels and five representative AI edit operations, covering four domains while preserving complete authorship provenance at multiple granularities. The benchmark supports comprehensive evaluation with 8 document-level detectors, 7 sentence-level detectors, and 2 fine-grained token/span-level detectors. Experiments reveal that AI-text detectability is governed not only by the proportion of AI-edited content, but also by edit operation, domain, and cumulative revision history. Interestingly, we notice that mixed-authorship intermediate versions are often harder to detect than both fully human and heavily AI-edited endpoints, exposing non-monotonic detection patterns missed by existing benchmarks. OpAI-Bench provides a controlled testbed for analyzing whether, when, and how AI-assisted writing becomes detectable under realistic progressive editing scenarios. Our code and benchmark are available at https://github.com/VILA-Lab/OpAI-Bench.

### [206] [Should Demand Models Incorporate Competitor Prices? Oblivious Learning and Algorithmic Collusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05363)
*Yuhang Wu,Assaf Zeevi*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究竞争市场中，定价算法是否应显式建模竞争对手价格。结果表明，忽略竞争对手（ oblivious）虽可能产生暂时的共谋模式，但随着学习推进这些模式会消散；而包含竞争对手信息（ informed）的策略在博弈中构成唯一纳什均衡，且能有效收敛到竞争性结果。因此，纳入竞争对手信息并配合充分的价格探索是更可靠的策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典学习理论认为忽略竞争对手会导致模型误设和效率损失，而近期算法共谋研究则表明战略性地忽略竞争对手价格可能促进共谋并提升利润。本文旨在厘清这一矛盾，研究在竞争市场中定价算法是否应建模竞争对手价格。

Method: 构建一个多卖家重复定价的竞争市场模型，需求未知且带有噪声。卖家通过迭代最小二乘法估计需求，分为两类：informed（纳入竞争对手价格）和oblivious（忽略竞争对手价格）。进行理论分析和博弈均衡刻画。

Result: 1) oblivious卖家需比垄断者更激进地探索以补偿信息损失；2) 所有卖家均为oblivious时，充分探索下价格收敛到竞争性结果，探索衰减时出现连续统的伪均衡；3) 价格轨迹存在" excursion"现象，产生暂时性共谋模式但随学习消散；4) 混合市场中informed卖家收益严格高于oblivious卖家；5) all-informed市场是唯一纳什均衡，价格高效收敛到竞争性结果。

Conclusion: 共谋模式不具有鲁棒性，不能通过oblivious建模来维持。纳入竞争对手信息并配合充分的价格探索是竞争市场中卖家更可靠的策略。

Abstract: On a platform with many sellers, should a pricing algorithm explicitly model competitors' prices when learning demand? Classical learning arguments suggest an affirmative answer: ignoring competitors induces model misspecification and inefficiency. In contrast, recent work on algorithmic collusion suggests that strategic obliviousness -- deliberately ignoring competitor prices -- may facilitate collusive outcomes and improve profits. We study this modeling choice in a stylized competitive market with unknown noisy demand, in which multiple sellers repeatedly set prices and estimate demand via iterated least squares, and either incorporate competitors' prices into their demand models (informed) or ignore them (oblivious). We first show that, relative to a monopolist, an oblivious seller in a competitive market must explore more aggressively to compensate for the loss of dynamic competitor information. Building on this insight, we characterize market dynamics when all sellers are oblivious and show that prices converge to the competitive outcome under sufficient exploration, while a continuum of pseudo-equilibria arises when exploration decays. Analyzing the resulting price trajectories, we uncover an excursion phenomenon that gives rise to transient collusive patterns that dissipate as learning progresses. In markets with both oblivious and informed sellers, the informed strictly out-earn the oblivious. Read as a strategy game, the modeling choice has a unique Nash equilibrium: the all-informed market, in which prices converge to the competitive outcome efficiently. Overall, our results indicate that collusive patterns are not robust and are not sustained by oblivious modeling; therefore, incorporating competitor information, together with sufficient price exploration, remains a reliable strategy for sellers in competitive markets.

</details>


### [207] [Exploring cooperation mechanisms via reinforcement learning in network common-pool resource games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05867)
*Yihang Qin,Lin Wang*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出图神经网络强化学习框架训练社会规划者，在网络公共池资源博弈中实现自适应资源分配，相比均等分配和比例分配，能同时提升合作水平、资源总量并降低不平等性，并将学到的策略蒸馏为可解释的混合分配机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有均等分配虽公平但削弱贡献激励导致效率低下，比例分配虽短期促进合作但会放大累积优势造成严重不平等，亟需一种能兼顾效率、公平与资源可持续性的分配机制。

Method: 构建网络公共池资源博弈模型，个体嵌入复杂网络并参与多个重叠局部资源池；采用图神经网络强化学习训练社会规划者，在不直接控制个体策略的前提下分配局部资源；在四种代表性网络拓扑下进行仿真，并将学到的策略蒸馏为资源依赖混合机制和度条件混合机制。

Result: 学习到的规划者在所有四种网络拓扑下均比均等分配和比例分配基准维持了更高的合作水平、更高的平均累积资源，同时降低了不平等性。

Conclusion: 有效的资源分配应同时适应当地资源状态和个体结构位置，强化学习策略搜索可为网络化资源共享系统的机制设计提供可解释的路径。

Abstract: Sustaining cooperation in resource-constrained populations requires allocation mechanisms that balance individual incentives, resource sustainability, and distributional fairness. This paper proposes a network common-pool resource game in which individuals are embedded in complex networks, participate in multiple overlapping local resource pools, and face endogenous resource constraints during strategy evolution. Within this framework, we first examine two representative allocation mechanisms, equal allocation and proportional allocation. The results show that equal allocation produces fair but inefficient outcomes by weakening contribution incentives, whereas proportional allocation can temporarily promote cooperation but amplifies accumulated advantages and leads to severe inequality. To overcome these limitations, we develop a graph neural network-based reinforcement learning framework in which a learned social planner allocates local pool resources without directly controlling individual strategies. Simulation results under four representative network topologies show that the learned planner sustains higher cooperation levels and average accumulated resources, and reduces inequality compared with the baselines. Furthermore, we interpret the learned policy and distill it into two simpler mechanisms: a resource-dependent mixture mechanism for regular networks and a degree-conditioned mixture mechanism for heterogeneous networks. These mechanisms reveal that effective allocation should adapt to both local resource states and structural positions, providing an interpretable route from reinforcement learning policy search to mechanism design in networked resource-sharing systems.

### [208] [Metric Facility Assignment with Partial Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05905)
*Vasilis Gkatzelis,Hasti Karimi,Emma Rewinski,Maziar Shamsipour,Alexandros A. Voudouris*

Main category: cs.GT

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在仅有部分信息的条件下（如代理人对设施的序数偏好），传统方法只能达到失真界3。本文试图探索引入更多信息类型（审批偏好和设施间距离）是否能降低失真界。

Method: 针对ORD、APP、DIST三种信息类型的不同组合，设计确定性指派算法，并推导其失真界（distortion）的紧致上下界。

Result: APP+DIST组合下得到紧致失真界1+√2（适用于一般度量空间）；ORD+APP+DIST组合下得到紧致失真界2；仅用ORD时最优界为3。

Conclusion: 引入除序数偏好外的额外信息（审批偏好和设施间距离）可以显著降低指派问题的失真界，且部分结果对一般度量空间也成立。

Abstract: We study an assignment problem where a set of agents and a set of facilities lie on a line metric. The goal is to compute an assignment of agents to facilities to approximately minimize the social cost (the total distance of agents from their assigned facilities) given only partial information regarding the metric. Unlike previous work which focused solely on algorithms with access to the ordinal preferences of the agents over the facilities (ORD), we also consider the value of information regarding approval preferences (APP), and inter-facility distances (DIST). For different combinations of these three information types, we establish tight bounds on the distortion of deterministic algorithms, showing that it is possible to improve over the optimal bound of $3$ that can be achieved using only ORD information. Among other results, we show a tight bound of $1+\sqrt{2}$ for APP+DIST which holds even for general metrics, and a tight bound of $2$ for ORD+APP+DIST.

### [209] [Revenue Guarantees of No-Swap-Regret Dynamics in First Price Auctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06085)
*Anders Bo Ipsen,Stratis Skoulakis*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究离散一级价格拍卖中近似相关均衡的收益，证明了任何ε-近似相关均衡的收益至少为v₂ - Θ(1/k) - Θ(εk²)，其中v₂为第二高估值。这是首次给出无交换遗憾投标人在一级价格拍卖中收益的多项式收敛速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为理解无交换遗憾投标人在一级价格拍卖中的收益表现，建立收益的下界和收敛速率。

Method: 通过理论分析离散竞价空间（B = {0, 1/k, ..., 1-1/k, 1}）中ε-近似相关均衡的收益下界，推导出收益与离散化粒度k、近似程度ε及第二高估值v₂的关系。

Result: 任何ε-近似相关均衡的收益至少为v₂ - Θ(1/k) - Θ(εk²)；当投标人具有最优交换遗憾O(√(kT))时，时间平均收益至少为v₂ - Θ(1/k) - Θ(ε)，达到该结果需要O(k⁵/ε²)轮。

Conclusion: 首次建立了一级价格拍卖中无交换遗憾投标人收益的多项式收敛速率，为理解拍卖博弈中学习算法的均衡收益提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the revenue of approximate correlated equilibrium in discrete first price auctions - the set of allowable bids is $\mathcal{B} = \{0, 1/k, \dots, 1 - 1/k, 1\}$ for some $k \in \mathbb{N}$. We show that the revenue of any $ε$-approximate correlated equilibrium is at least $v_2 - Θ(1/k)- Θ(εk^2)$, where $v_2 \geq 0$ is the second-highest valuation. Our results establish the first polynomial convergence rates on the revenue generated by no-swap regret bidders in first-price auctions.
  For instance, if bidders admit the optimal swap regret of $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{k T})$, then the time-averaged revenue is at least $v_2 - Θ(1/k) - Θ(ε)$ after $\mathcal{O}(k^5/ε^2)$ rounds.

</details>


### [210] [Regret Minimization in Single-Dimensional Contract-Design with Binary Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06125)
*Riccardo Poiani,Martino Bernasconi,Andrea Celli*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了在线主-代理问题中，委托人在无法观测代理人行动的情况下，仅通过可观测的产出结果学习最优合约。针对二元行动和单维代理人类型，在对抗性类型序列下获得了与产出数量无关的Θ(T^{2/3})遗憾界，在固定隐藏类型下获得了Õ(√T)的紧界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典主-代理问题通常假设委托人完全了解代理人的成本结构等信息，但实际中委托人往往对这些信息一无所知。本文旨在探索在不了解代理人类型且无法观测其行动的情况下，委托人如何通过与多个代理人重复交互来自适应地学习最优合约。

Method: 针对对抗性类型序列：1) 将问题约简为一维阈值优化问题；2) 采用非均匀离散化处理问题的非Lipschitz性质。针对固定隐藏类型：采用"探索-然后-提交"策略，先通过随机二分搜索近似学习隐藏类型，再提交一个"鲁棒化"的近优合约。

Result: 对抗性类型序列下得到紧的Θ(T^{2/3})遗憾界，且该速率与产出数量m完全无关；固定单一隐藏类型下得到紧的Õ(√T)遗憾界。

Conclusion: 本文给出了在线主-代理问题中学习最优合约的第一个严格理论保证，揭示了不同代理类型序列下可达到的最优学习速率，为合约设计中的在线学习提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study principal-agent problems in which a principal commits to an outcome-dependent payment scheme (i.e., a contract) in order to induce an agent to take a costly action leading to a favorable outcome. We consider the online extension of the classical (one-shot) principal-agent problem, in which the principal repeatedly interacts with agents by proposing contracts over multiple rounds. The principal has no information about the agents and, crucially, does not observe their actions. As a result, the principal must learn an optimal contract using only the realized outcomes observed at each round. We focus on the setting with binary actions and single-dimensional agent types, where the agent's private type represents their cost per unit-of-effort. For adversarial-type sequences, we provide tight $Θ(T^{2/3})$ regret guarantees. Remarkably, this rate is completely independent of the number of outcomes $m$. The upper bound is based on two key components: 1) a reduction to a one-dimensional threshold optimization problem and 2) a non-uniform discretization to handle the non-Lipschitz nature of the problem. Moreover, in the case of a single (fixed) hidden type, we show that it is possible to improve the rates and provide a tight $\widetildeΘ(\sqrt{T})$ regret bound. Our algorithm is based on an explore-then-commit strategy where we first approximately learn the hidden type via a stochastic binary search, and then we commit to a ``robustified'' near-optimal contract.

</details>


### [211] [A Unified Framework for Uniform-Price Resource Allocation Mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06151)
*Ioannis Caragiannis,Dimitris Fotakis,Stratis Skoulakis*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的资源分配机制设计框架，在保持Kelly机制比例分配和统一定价简洁性的同时，通过插值于Kelly机制与一价拍卖之间的机制族，显著提升了效率（可达完全效率）并提供了相对于VCG机制的收益保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可分割资源分配机制中，Kelly比例机制虽然简洁但效率有限；后续改进机制虽提升了社会福利，却牺牲了简单性（引入复杂分配规则或反直觉的支付方式）。因此，亟需一种既能保持Kelly机制简洁性（比例分配+统一定价）又能提升效率与收益保证的统一框架。

Method: 提出一个统一框架，设计了一族介于Kelly机制与一价拍卖之间的机制。这些机制保持比例式分配和统一定价（uniform pricing）的简洁特性，通过参数化设计在极端之间插值。

Result: 该机制族在均衡状态下严格提升了Kelly机制的效率保证，甚至可实现完全效率（full efficiency）；同时提供了相对于VCG机制（Vickrey-Clarke-Groves）的收益保证（revenue guarantees）。

Conclusion: 在保持比例分配和统一定价简洁性的前提下，通过统一框架设计的插值机制族能够在不牺牲简单性的同时，同时实现效率与收益的双重改进。

Abstract: Mechanisms for allocating a divisible resource among strategic agents have been widely studied. The prominent paradigm is the proportional (Kelly) mechanism, which elicits a scalar bid per agent, allocates the resource proportionally, and charges payments equal to the bids. Follow-up mechanisms improve social welfare, but sacrifice simplicity by introducing complex allocation rules or unintuitive payments.
  We introduce a unified framework for designing simple resource allocation mechanisms with proportional-style allocations and uniform pricing. Our framework yields a family of mechanisms that interpolate between the Kelly mechanism and the first-price auction. These mechanisms strictly improve upon Kelly's efficiency guarantees, even achieving full efficiency in equilibrium, while also providing revenue guarantees relative to the VCG mechanism.

Conclusion: 该工作为多值效用市场中的HZ均衡计算提供了首个理论保证的近似算法，展现了效用分层技术在机制设计中的潜力。

### [213] [Simultaneous EF1 and approximate MMS allocations for submodular valuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06451)
*Uriel Feige,Assaf Fine*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了在将不可分割物品分配给平等权利的代理人时，同时满足基于份额的公平概念（ρ-MMS）和基于比较的公平概念（EF1/EFL）的分配方案，特别是在子模估值（更一般的函数类）下证明了这种同时满足的可能性，而此前仅在可加估值下已知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两类公平概念（份额型如MMS、比较型如EF）在一般条件下无法相互提供良好保证，因此需要设计能够同时满足两类概念的分配方案，以在更广泛的估值函数类（子模估值）中实现这一目标。

Method: 通过理论分析和算法设计，在子模估值函数下构造同时满足ρ-MMS（ρ为常数）和EF1（以及EFL）的分配方案。

Result: 在子模估值下，成功设计出同时满足常数ρ的ρ-MMS和EF1/EFL的分配方案，将此前仅在可加估值下成立的结果推广到更一般的子模估值类。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了两类公平概念在更一般估值函数下的交叉保证空白，证明了在子模估值下仍可同时实现份额型与比较型公平。

Abstract: There are two common classes of fairness notions that are considered when allocating $m$ indivisible items to $n$ agents of equal entitlements. One is that of share-based fairness notions, with the maximin share (MMS) and its relaxations to $ρ$-MMS being prominent representatives of this class. The other is that of comparison-based fairness notions, with envy-freeness (EF) and its relaxations such as EF1 being prominent representatives of this class. In general, no class offers good guarantees for the other class. In this work, we design allocations that simultaneously satisfy notions from both classes, and specifically, are $ρ$-MMS for constant $ρ$ and EF1 (in fact, also EFL). Such results were previously known when agents have additive valuations, and we prove such results for the more general class of submodular valuations.

</details>


### [214] [DNQ: Deep Nash Q-Network for Partially Observable n-Player Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06480)
*Qintong Xie,Edward Koh,Xavier Cadet,Peter Chin*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出DNQ框架，通过求解器在环的均衡监督方法训练竞标智能体，在共享约束和重复交互的多智能体同时竞标场景中，交替进行轨迹收集、批评者收益估计、均衡计算和策略模仿，实验表明成对公式相比精确公式在更多智能体场景下更具可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中的竞争系统（如拍卖、资源分配、安全竞争）需要多个决策者在共享约束、有限信息和重复交互下同时行动，但现有方法难以有效训练此类场景下的竞标智能体。

Method: 提出DNQ框架，采用求解器在环的均衡监督方式：在每次访问状态时，共享批评者预测成对收益矩阵或精确N玩家收益张量，外部求解器计算均衡策略，智能体通过最小化其掩码策略与求解器导出的均衡目标之间的KL散度进行训练。

Result: 成对公式相比精确公式大幅降低了均衡求解成本和训练时间，可扩展到更多智能体数量，而精确公式在联合博弈规模增长时变得计算上不可行。

Conclusion: 在重复竞争环境中，存在战略保真度与可扩展性之间的权衡：成对方法牺牲部分战略精度换取可扩展性，而精确方法虽战略保真度高但计算代价过大。

Abstract: Many real-world competitive systems require multiple decision-makers to act simultaneously under shared constraints, limited information, and repeated interaction, as in auctions, resource allocation, and security competition. We study multi-turn simultaneous bidding as a controlled testbed for such problems and propose DNQ, a solver-in-the-loop equilibrium supervision framework for training bidding agents. DNQ alternates between trajectory collection, critic-based payoff estimation, equilibrium computation, and policy imitation. At each visited state, a shared critic predicts either pairwise payoff matrices or an exact N-player payoff tensor, an external solver computes equilibrium strategies, and the agents are trained by minimizing the KL divergence between their masked policies and the solver-derived equilibrium targets. We focus on a scalable pairwise formulation that greatly reduces equilibrium-solving cost and training time compared with the exact formulation, while the shared critic amortizes payoff learning across agents and states. Experiments compare the pairwise and exact variants using critic loss, policy entropy, bidding resource usage, and training cost, showing that the pairwise method scales to larger numbers of agents, whereas the exact method becomes computationally impractical as the joint game grows. These results illustrate the trade-off between strategic fidelity and scalability in repeated competitive environments.

</details>

### [215] [A Comprehensive Survey on Semantic Communication in Non-Terrestrial Networks: Architectures, Methodologies, and Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05216)
*Loc X. Nguyen,Avi Deb Raha,Huy Q. Le,Zhu Han,Eui-Nam Huh,Choong Seon Hong*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本综述系统论证了语义通信（SemCom）与非地面网络（NTN）的天然互补性：NTN面临路径损耗大、时延高、多普勒频移大、能算受限等瓶颈，而SemCom的任务导向极致压缩、深度联合源信道编码、生成式AI重构等特性恰好能逐一应对这些挑战。论文沿NTN平台、语义方法论、支撑技术三个维度组织文献，并深入分析了卫星、无人机/高空平台、空天地一体化系统，最后提出了基础模型应用、能量感知调度、量子辅助语义通信等未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非地面网络（NTN）虽然被公认为第六代无线网络的关键使能技术，但其架构面临路径损耗、传播时延、多普勒频移、可见窗口受限、星载能算预算紧张等多重固有缺陷。现有的通信技术难以同时应对这些相互耦合的挑战，因此亟需寻找一种天然适配NTN物理特性的新型通信范式。

Method: 论文首先采用"问题-方案"配对分析框架，逐一将NTN的每个限制映射到SemCom的对应设计选择上；随后从NTN平台类型（卫星、无人机/HAPS、空天地一体化）、语义方法论（语义编码、联合源信道编码、生成式AI）、支撑技术（机器学习、标准化）三个维度对现有文献进行系统分类；最后针对每个平台类型进行深入剖析。

Result: 发现NTN的每一个关键限制都能找到对应的SemCom技术解决方案：1）路径损耗→任务导向极致压缩降低带宽需求；2）低信噪比→深度联合源信道编码避免悬崖效应；3）雨衰/链路阻塞→生成式AI从稀疏信号中重构内容；4）长短时延→语义理解减少交互轮次；5）星载算力有限→轻量化语义模型适配边缘部署。

Conclusion: 语义通信与非地面网络存在结构性互补关系，两者结合有望成为6G全域覆盖的关键技术路径。未来开放问题包括：基础模型在星载环境的高效部署、能量感知的语义调度策略、以及面向深空通信的量子辅助语义通信方案。现有标准（如3GPP NTN）尚未充分纳入语义通信相关设计，存在显著标准化缺口。

Abstract: The sixth-generation wireless networks are envisioned to deliver ubiquitous, seamless, and intelligent connectivity that reaches far beyond the limits of terrestrial infrastructure. Non-terrestrial networks (NTNs) are central to this vision, extending coverage to underserved regions, remote terrain, and disaster zones that terrestrial deployment cannot economically reach. However, NTN architecture faces numerous limitations: severe path loss over long distances, long propagation delays, large and time-varying Doppler shifts, limited visibility windows, and tight on-board energy and computing budgets. Semantic communication (SemCom), which conveys the meaning of data rather than its raw bit-level representation, is unusually well matched to these conditions: extreme compression rate for task-oriented eases bandwidth scarcity, deep joint source-channel coding prevents the cliff effect due to low signal-to-noise ratio, and generative-AI reconstructs content from sparse cues that survive rain-faded or blocked links. This observation, that each NTN limitation maps onto a SemCom property that addresses it, motivates our survey. We first walk through the NTN limitations one by one, pairing each with the SemCom design choices that complement it, then we organize the literature along three axes: the NTN platform, the semantic methodology, and the supporting techniques, and follow this with platform-by-platform deep dives on satellite-centric, UAV/HAPS-centric, and integrated SAGIN systems. The survey concludes by identifying open research problems, gaps in existing standards, and future directions, including the application of foundation models, energy-aware scheduling, and quantum-assisted SemCom for deep space communication.

</details>


### [216] [Bounded Deep Unfolding for Joint Beamforming and Scheduling in Multi-Cell MIMO Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05246)
*Jiansheng Li,Shuqi Chai,Fan Xu,Kaiming Shen,Guangxu Zhu,Junting Chen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种联合深度展开框架（P-Net和K-Net），分别用于加速多小区MIMO下行链路中连续波束成形优化和离散资源块组调度，在保证收敛性的同时显著提升加权和速率并降低计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FastFP框架在多小区MIMO下行链路加权和速率最大化问题中，存在连续波束成形更新保守（使用固定松弛因子）以及离散RBG匹配阶段计算开销过高（匈牙利算法）两大瓶颈。

Method: 提出联合深度展开框架：1) P-Net：在FastFP解析更新方向基础上，学习一个自适应松弛因子并严格约束在保 ascent 区间内，加速优化轨迹同时保留单调改进和驻点收敛保证；2) K-Net：学习长视界优先级策略，指导低复杂度贪心分配替代匈牙利匹配。两网络均利用解析算法先验和循环参数共享，支持超训练时域推理。

Result: 大量仿真表明，所提联合框架相比传统模型驱动基线实现了更高的加权和速率和更快的执行时间，且在未见过的网络规模、天线配置和信道条件下无需重训练即可鲁棒泛化。

Conclusion: 将深度展开与模型驱动算法结合，通过可学习模块解决原算法保守性和高计算复杂度问题，能同时提升性能和效率，并具有良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: This paper investigates the joint resource block group (RBG) scheduling and beamforming optimization problem for weighted sum-rate (WSR) maximization in multi-cell multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) downlink networks. While the Fast Fractional Programming (FastFP) framework provides a reliable model-driven solution, it suffers from conservative continuous beamforming updates and prohibitive computational overhead during the discrete RBG matching phase. To address these bottlenecks, we propose a joint deep unfolding framework comprising two core modules: P-Net and K-Net. For continuous beamforming, P-Net learns an adaptive relaxation factor along the analytical FastFP update direction. By strictly constraining this factor within an ascent-preserving interval, P-Net accelerates the optimization trajectory while rigorously retaining monotonic improvement and stationary-point convergence guarantees. For discrete RBG scheduling, K-Net learns a long-horizon priority policy that guides a low-complexity greedy assignment, effectively preserving the assignment quality while bypassing the high complexity of Hungarian matching. Both networks leverage analytical algorithmic priors and utilize recurrent parameter sharing, enabling flexible inference beyond the training horizon. Extensive simulations demonstrate that the proposed joint framework achieves higher WSR and faster execution times than conventional model-driven baselines, while generalizing robustly across unseen network scales, antenna configurations, and channel conditions without retraining.

### [218] [Unlocking Exponential and Unbounded Robust Gains in Shannon Capacity of Classical Multiple Access Channels with Causal CSIT via Quantum Entanglement Assistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05412)
*Yuhang Yao,Syed A. Jafar*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文证明，在发送端具有因果信道状态信息（CSIT）的经典多址接入信道中，量子纠缠辅助可以带来乘法级容量增益：该增益随用户数K呈指数增长，且随状态字母表大小增长而无界。即使只有少量用户和小字母表（如二进制输入/输出/状态），增益仍十分显著（K=5时大于21倍，K=7时大于88倍），且在量子资源有噪声（如每个纠缠量子比特以约30%概率完全退极化）时仍保持指数级优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前量子纠缠辅助带来的香农容量增益非常有限（不到6%），引发了一个根本性疑问：量子纠缠是否可能带来大幅容量增益？本文旨在探究是否存在场景下量子纠缠辅助能提供远超传统小增益的容量优势。

Method: 理论分析：针对经典K用户多址接入信道，在发送端具有因果CSI的条件下，构建纠缠辅助的通信模型；通过信息论容量界分析，推导纠缠辅助容量与经典容量的比值（乘法增益），并分析增益随用户数K和状态字母表大小的缩放行为；进一步分析纠缠资源存在噪声（独立退极化）时增益的鲁棒性。

Result: 1) 量子纠缠辅助可提供随用户数K指数增长的乘法容量增益；2) 在固定用户数K=3、二进制输入/输出时，增益随状态字母表大小增长而无界；3) 二进制输入/输出/状态下，K=5时增益>21倍，K=7时>88倍；4) 即使每个纠缠量子比特以约30%概率完全退极化，指数级容量优势仍然保持。

Conclusion: 量子纠缠辅助能在特定通信场景（发送端具有因果CSI的MAC）中带来巨大且鲁棒的容量增益，否定了此前认为纠缠辅助增益有限的认知，为量子辅助通信的理论极限提供了新认识。

Abstract: Quantum entanglement assistance is known to improve the Shannon capacity of classical communication networks but the largest gains noted thus far are rather modest (less than 6%), motivating the question: are large capacity gains ever possible? It is shown in this work that in the presence of causal channel state information at the transmitters, quantum entanglement assistance provides a multiplicative capacity advantage that grows exponentially with the number of users K for certain classical K-user multiple access channels with fixed size (binary) alphabet for inputs, outputs and states. Similarly, in the presence of causal channel state information at the transmitters, quantum entanglement assistance is shown to provide a multiplicative capacity advantage that is unbounded as the size of the state alphabet grows, while the number of users (K=3) and the input and output alphabet (binary) are held fixed. Even with only a few users and small alphabet sizes, substantial multiplicative gains in capacity are found, e.g., with binary inputs, outputs and states, multiplicative gains by factors exceeding 21 and 88 are noted with K=5 and K=7 users, respectively. The gains are robust in the sense that they persist even with noisy quantum resources, e.g., an exponential (in K) capacity advantage from quantum entanglement assistance remains available even if each entangled qubit independently depolarizes completely with probability $\approx$ 30%. The gains are based on quantum entanglement assistance provided only to the transmitters.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出新的唯一重建充分条件，综合考虑读取次数和读取间距离；并设计相应的理论分析框架和高效重建算法。

Result: 建立了新的唯一重建充分条件，并给出了对应的理论分析结果和高效重建算法。

Abstract: In the sequence reconstruction problem, a codeword $\x$ is transmitted through several identical channels where each channel produces a noisy read of $\x$, and the problem is to analyze how to uniquely reconstruct $\x$ based on these noisy reads. Levenshtein has studied the minimum number of reads which guarantees unique reconstruction of $\x$, which is one sufficient condition for unique reconstruction. In this paper, we move on to a different perspective and propose a new framework for unique reconstruction. Our new sufficient condition for unique reconstruction takes both the number of reads and the distances among the reads into consideration. We offer both theoretical analysis and corresponding efficient reconstruction algorithms for our reconstruction framework.

### [220] [Robust Repair of Reed-Solomon Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05573)
*Wilton Kim,Stanislav Kruglik,Gaojun Luo,Han Mao Kiah*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究在低通信带宽下，针对Reed-Solomon码中单个擦除的鲁棒修复问题，即在Guruswami-Wootters迹修复框架下，当辅助节点给出错误响应时如何正确修复故障节点。通过将下载迹视为一种码（修复迹码），利用多项式零系数与分圆陪集的关系推导了允许纠正给定数量错误迹的维度上界及最小距离下界。针对q=2情形，利用分圆陪集代表元的显式公式获得了单错误纠正的精确最优维度界。提出了两种高效鲁棒修复方案：第一种达到BCH界保证的纠错能力；第二种基于字符和达到更强界，以额外n倍计算复杂度为代价容忍更多错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Reed-Solomon码的修复方案大多假设辅助节点响应无差错，但实际存储系统中辅助节点可能返回错误信息。如何在低通信带宽下实现鲁棒修复是一个重要问题。

Method: 将下载迹集合视为修复迹码，通过分析多项式零系数与分圆陪集的关系推导纠错能力上界。针对q=2情形利用分圆陪集代表元显式公式得到精确最优界。提出两种修复方案：方案一基于BCH界，方案二基于字符和达到更强纠错能力。

Result: 推导了允许纠正e个错误迹的维度k的上界，以及作为k函数的最小距离下界。对q=2情形给出了单错误纠正的精确最优维度界。方案一达到BCH界保证的纠错能力；方案二容忍更多错误，但计算复杂度增加n倍。

Conclusion: 本文在Guruswami-Wootters迹修复框架下系统研究了Reed-Solomon码的鲁棒修复问题，为低通信带宽下的纠错修复提供了理论界和实用方案。

Abstract: We study the problem of robust repair of a single erasure in Reed--Solomon codes under low communication bandwidth. Focusing on the Guruswami--Wootters trace repair framework, we investigate whether a failed node can be correctly repaired in the presence of erroneous responses from helper nodes. Equivalently, we view the collection of downloaded traces as a code, which we call the repair-trace code. By characterizing the zero coefficients of the associated polynomial in terms of cyclotomic cosets, we derive upper bounds on the dimension $k$ that allow correction of a given number of erroneous traces $e$, as well as lower bounds on the minimum distance as a function of $k$. For the case $q=2$, we exploit explicit formulas for cyclotomic coset representatives to obtain the exact optimal dimension bound for single-error correction. We also propose two efficient robust repair schemes. Our first scheme achieves the error-correction capability guaranteed by the BCH bound. To approach a stronger bound based on character sums, we develop a second scheme that tolerates more errors at the cost of an additional factor $n$ in computational complexity.

</details>


### [221] [Energy Efficiency Optimization for Rotatable Antenna-Enabled Uplink NOMA Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05600)
*Yixuan Li,Jun Wang,Hongbo Xu,Ji Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究可旋转天线（RA）增强的上行非正交多址接入（NOMA）系统，通过联合优化接收波束赋形、用户功率分配和RA旋转来实现能效最大化，并提出基于块坐标下降的算法，仿真验证了所提方案的能效优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在RA-enabled NOMA系统中，如何通过联合优化接收波束赋形、功率分配和天线旋转来最大化系统能效，同时服务地面和空中用户。

Method: 采用块坐标下降（BCD）算法，将问题分解为三个子问题：接收波束赋形通过最小均方误差（MMSE）准则更新，功率分配通过分数规划（FP）处理，RA旋转通过逐次凸近似（SCA）求解。

Result: 数值结果表明，所提出的RA-NOMA方案在能效方面优于多个基准方案。

Conclusion: 将可旋转天线与NOMA相结合能够有效提升上行通信系统的能效表现，联合优化框架具备可行性和优越性。

Abstract: This paper investigates a rotatable antenna (RA)-enabled uplink non-orthogonal multiple access (NOMA) system, where a base station equipped with multiple independently RAs serves both ground and aerial users. Specifically, we formulate an energy efficiency (EE) maximization problem by jointly optimizing receive beamforming, user power allocation, and RA rotation. To make the problem tractable, a new block coordinate descent-based algorithm is developed, in which the receive beamforming is updated via the minimum mean square error criterion, while the power allocation and RA rotation are handled by fractional programming and successive convex approximation. Numerical results demonstrate the EE superiority of the proposed RA-NOMA scheme over several benchmarks.

</details>


### [222] [Automated Proving of Shannon-Type Entropy Inequalities via Fine-Tuned Language Models and Guided Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05729)
*Shing Yin Wong,Shaocheng Liu,Linqi Song,Amin Gohari,Cheuk Ting Li*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究小规模语言模型（0.6B-1.7B参数）在证明香农型熵不等式中的自动化能力，通过微调原子证明步骤并结合引导式束搜索，在10-15变量的60条不等式测试集上，0.6B模型达到85%证明成功率，远超GPT-5.5（1.7%）和Psitip（33.3%）。消融实验表明4096 token非偏斜训练分布最优，束搜索评分启发式至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 香农型熵不等式证明是信息论中的基础任务，需要构造已知约束的非平凡线性组合，这是一个随着随机变量数量增加而扩展性极差的组合搜索问题。现有方法（如Psitip）和大型通用模型（GPT-5.5）在此任务上表现不佳，亟需更高效的自动化方法。

Method: 采用小规模语言模型（0.6B-1.7B参数），在原子证明步骤上进行微调，结合引导式束搜索（guided beam search）进行自动推理。通过消融实验系统研究训练上下文长度（4096 vs 8192 tokens）和数据分布（n=9偏斜 vs 非偏斜）的影响。

Result: 0.6B微调模型在60条不等式测试集（n=10-15变量）上，结合树搜索达到85%证明成功率。GPT-5.5零样本提示仅解决1.7%，Psitip解决33.3%。4096 token非偏斜训练分布表现最优，扩展上下文和偏斜数据无额外收益。束评分启发式至关重要（消融后成功率从83%降至23%）。

Conclusion: 小规模语言模型通过针对性微调和适当搜索策略，在特定数学推理任务（熵不等式证明）上可以显著超越大型通用模型和专用工具，且模型规模并非越大越好，训练数据分布和搜索启发式对性能影响更为关键。

Abstract: Proving Shannon-type entropy inequalities is a fundamental task in information theory that often requires constructing non-trivial linear combinations of known constraints, which is a combinatorial search problem that scales poorly with the number of random variables. We investigate whether small-scale large language models (0.6B--1.7B parameters), fine-tuned on atomic proof steps and combined with guided beam search, can automate this process. On a held-out test set of 60 inequalities spanning n=10 to 15 variables, our 0.6B fine-tuned model achieves an 85\% proof success rate with tree search. GPT-5.5 solves 1.7\% samples under zero-shot prompting while Psitip solves 33.3\% samples. A systematic ablation study across training context length (4096 vs.\ 8192 tokens) and data distribution (n=9-skewed vs not skewed) reveals that a 4096-token not skewed training distribution yields the best performance, with extended context and skewed data providing no marginal benefit. We further identify two dominant failure modes -- format failures and step quality degradation -- and verify that the beam-scoring heuristic is essential via a controlled ablation (random scoring reduces success from 83\% to 23\%).

</details>


### [223] [Compositional Boundaries for Density Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05871)
*Ratan Bahadur Thapa,Ali Darijani,Jürgen Beyerer,Steffen Staab*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了分布式不确定性管理系统中概率密度加权融合的代数组合性问题，证明了在连续二元融合规则中，阶不变的分层执行唯一对应于归一化加权线性池化；而基于f-散度的端点平衡方法由于局部几何特性导致平方根有效权重，因此无法实现调度无关的融合；高斯混合模型进一步验证了精确融合与逐步压缩在组合性上的本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式不确定性管理系统沿聚合树组合局部概率模型时，最终密度应取决于加权源而非中间节点的融合顺序。本文旨在从代数组合性角度研究这一需求，回答何时局部融合规则可以分层执行且保持阶不变。

Method: 建立了局部段值融合规则的组合性边界；在连续二元规则类中刻画了阶不变分层执行的条件；通过二次展开分析了端点到候选f-散度平衡的局部几何特性；利用高斯混合模型验证了理论在有限模型类中的表现。

Result: 阶不变分层执行唯一对应于归一化加权线性池化；f-散度平衡的二次膨胀导致平方根有效权重，使得成对可解性不足以实现调度无关融合；高斯混合模型中精确融合具有组合性，而逐步压缩仅在未归一化分量测度满足同余条件时才具有组合性。

Conclusion: 精确的调度无关融合与全局聚合目标及局部近似启发式之间存在本质区别，为分布式不确定性融合系统的设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Distributed uncertainty-management systems often combine local probabilistic models along aggregation trees chosen by communication, privacy, or scheduling constraints. The final density should depend on the weighted sources, not on the particular order in which intermediate nodes combine them. We study this requirement as an algebraic compositionality problem for binary fusion of weighted probability densities. The central question is when a local fusion rule can be executed hierarchically while remaining order-invariant. We establish a compositional boundary for local segment-valued fusion rules. Within the class of continuous binary rules with additive output weights and weight-only coefficients, order-invariant hierarchical execution characterizes normalized weighted linear pooling; norm-induced segment balancing realizes the corresponding coefficient. Smooth endpoint-to-candidate $f$-divergence balancing has a different local geometry: its quadratic expansion induces square-root effective weights, showing why pairwise solvability alone is insufficient for schedule-independent fusion. We show that this obstruction is local to endpoint-to-candidate binary balancing, whereas global divergence barycenters retain additive-weight local limits. Finally, Gaussian mixtures show how the same issue appears in finite model classes: exact fusion is compositional, whereas stepwise compression is compositional only under a congruence condition on unnormalized component measures. These results distinguish exact schedule-independent fusion from global aggregation objectives and local approximation heuristics.

</details>


### [224] [Double-Directional Wireless Channel Modeling Using Statistics-Aided Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05993)
*Richmond Boamah,Ferdous Pervej*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机性和确定性信道模型以及机器学习解决方案在生成未来信道实现时，往往局限于短时间跨度，缺乏统计显著性；同时多径分量数量随空间和时间变化，传统ML需要固定输入输出形状，难以处理变长MPC问题。

Method: 首先选择前M个多径分量（M远小于总MPC数），构建可学习图结构；然后训练混合TimesNet-TimeFilter（TNTF）模型；最后采用信道统计辅助的训练方法，使得生成的未来前M个DD信道实现与实际完整时变DD信道统计特性相匹配。

Result: 在合成随机信道模型和确定性射线追踪数据集上进行仿真验证，结果表明所提方法优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: 通过固定子集选择与统计匹配训练的结合，有效解决了变长MPC和短时间跨度问题，为双方向信道建模提供了一种新的ML解决方案。

Abstract: The double-directional (DD) wireless channel model is important for realistic system design since it provides complete propagation information. While stochastic and deterministic channel models are widely adopted, and existing machine learning (ML) solutions mostly aim to align future channel realizations, these solutions are often limited to short time spans that may not be statistically significant. Moreover, because the number of multi-path components (MPCs) varies with spatial and temporal variation of the receiver (RX) and/or interacting objects (IOs), typical ML solutions that require fixed, predefined input and output shapes fall short. To curb these limitations, we propose a statistics-aided ML solution that relies on a fixed subset of MPCs selection. More specifically, we first select top-$M$ MPCs, where $M\in\mathbb{Z}^+$ is much smaller than the total number of MPCs, and construct learnable graphs to train our proposed hybrid TimesNet-TimeFilter (TNTF) model. We then use a channel statistics-aided training method to generate future top-M DD channel realizations such that the statistics calculated from these realizations matches closely with those of the actual statistics from the complete time-varying DD channel realizations. We validate the proposed solution using extensive simulations on both synthetic stochastic channel model (SCM)-based and deterministic ray-tracing-based datasets, and demonstrate its effectiveness relative to state-of-the-art baselines.

</details>


### [225] [Adapting Diffusion Language Models for Lossless Pixel-Level Image Transmission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06273)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无损像素级图像传输是超越语义通信的基本范式，因为精确恢复需要同时准确的符号概率建模和可靠的信道传输，现有方法在效率和性能上存在不足。

Method: 提出离散扩散模型（DDM）作为源编解码器，采用扩散语言模型进行像素令牌恢复，在双向注意力下执行同步反向算术编码；引入Halton引导的去噪顺序、掩码率感知的余弦调度和轻量温度校准模块。

Result: 在CIFAR10、DIV2K-LR-X4和Kodak数据集上，AWGN和瑞利衰落信道下，DDM-SSCC在精确恢复性能上优于代表性无损和语义通信基线，消融实验验证了各模块的有效性。

Conclusion: DDM-SSCC框架有效结合了离散扩散模型与无损算术编码，通过渐进恢复和双向上下文实现了更优的无损图像传输性能。

Abstract: Lossless pixel-level image transmission is a fundamental regime beyond semantic communications, because exact recovery requires both accurate symbol probability modeling and reliable delivery over noisy channels. This paper proposes DDM-SSCC, a discrete-diffusion-model-based separate source-channel coding framework for lossless image transmission. Different from raster-order autoregressive coding, the proposed source codec adapts a diffusion language model to pixel-token restoration and performs synchronized reverse arithmetic coding under bidirectional attention, allowing multiple masked tokens to be coded within one reverse denoising step. This progressive restoration process also yields a more favorable source representation for noisy transmission, since newly restored tokens can serve as bidirectional context in subsequent denoising steps. To bridge the gap between generation-oriented masked denoising and lossless arithmetic coding, we further introduce a Halton-guided denoising order, a mask-ratio-aware cosine schedule, and a lightweight temperature calibration module. These designs respectively improve spatial coverage, adapt the denoising pace to context reliability, and calibrate the probability tables used by arithmetic coding. Experiments on CIFAR10, DIV2K-LR-X4, and Kodak over additive white Gaussian noise and Rayleigh fading channels show that DDM-SSCC achieves better exact-recovery performance than representative lossless and semantic communication baselines, while ablation studies verify the effectiveness of the proposed denoising order, schedule, and calibration modules.
