### [226] [A Spherical Stochastic Geometry Framework for Patrol-Based HAPs Network: Coverage and Energy Efficiency Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06307)
*Mohammad Taha Shah,Mohamed-Slim Alouini*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文建立了高空平台站（HAPs）网络的随机几何分析框架，提出了两种球面小圆环Cox过程模型（SCR-PCP和SCR-BCP），推导了关键空间统计量与覆盖概率表达式，并引入覆盖能效（CEE）指标以实现巡逻半径的能量最优设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出两种球面小圆环Cox过程模型：SCR-PCP（强度驱动，泊松点过程）和SCR-BCP（有限舰队，二项点过程）；2. 建立模型各向同性并推导最近锚点、最近环、最近HAPs距离分布及联合服务距离与服务环角分布；3. 基于最近HAPs关联策略，将聚合干扰分解为同环干扰与异环干扰，推导条件拉普拉斯变换与覆盖概率表达式；4. 集成稳态圆形飞行推进模型，定义覆盖能效（CEE）指标，推导最优巡逻半径的解析条件。

Result: 数值结果表明强度驱动型（SCR-PCP）与有限舰队型（SCR-BCP）部署存在本质差异；巡逻几何构型、平台密度与巡航速度需联合优化才能实现能效最优的HAPs运行。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架能够有效指导HAPs网络中巡逻轨迹的几何参数设计，在保证覆盖性能的同时最小化推进能耗，为实际部署提供了理论依据与优化条件。

Abstract: This paper develops a stochastic-geometry framework for high-altitude platform station (HAPs) networks in which platforms execute cyclic patrol trajectories anchored to designated service regions. We introduce two small-circle ring Cox process models on the spherical Earth. In the small-circle ring Poisson Cox process (SCR-PCP), platforms form one-dimensional Poisson point processes on localized patrol rings, whereas in the small-circle ring binomial Cox process (SCR-BCP), each ring contains a fixed number of uniformly distributed platforms. We establish the isotropy of both models and derive spatial statistics, including the distributions of the nearest-anchor, nearest-ring, and nearest-HAPs distances, together with the joint serving distance and serving ring angle distribution required for SCR-BCP analysis. Building on these results, we derive coverage probability expressions under nearest-HAPs association by decomposing aggregate interference into same-ring and other-ring components and characterizing their conditional Laplace transforms. To account for the flight dynamics of patrol-based HAPs, we integrate a steady circular flight propulsion model with the communication analysis and introduce a coverage energy efficiency (CEE) metric. This yields an analytical condition for the energy-optimal patrol radius that balances coverage performance against the propulsion cost of circular flight. Numerical results reveal fundamental differences between intensity-driven (SCR-PCP) and finite-fleet (SCR-BCP) deployments and demonstrate that patrol geometry, platform density, and cruising velocity should be jointly optimized to achieve energy-efficient HAPs operation.

Moreover, we study the necessary and sufficient conditions for a double cyclic code to be reversible and reversible-complement double cyclic code and with the help of these codes, we constructed DNA codes over $\mathbb F_4+u\mathbb F_4, u^2=0$. We also constructed some optimal codes to support our results.

### [228] [Full-Field Calibration of Coupled Thermomechanical Material Models at Finite Strain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05465)
*L. River Spencer,William D. Meador,Adrian Buganza Tepole,Brian N. Granzow,Jin Yang,Manuel K. Rausch,D. Thomas Seidl,Jan N. Fuhg*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种全场标定框架，利用边界位移、反作用力和温度数据，通过PDE约束优化和伴随灵敏度方法，从实验表面数据中推断热机械材料参数，无需体积观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热机械材料模型的标定面临变形、温度和力响应强耦合的挑战，且实验测量通常仅限于试件表面，因此需要一种仅利用表面可观测数据就能标定全场热机械参数的方法。

Method: 将正问题建模为基于亥姆霍兹自由能的近不可压缩热-超弹性问题，反问题构建为PDE约束优化问题并添加加权观测项；采用自动微分计算伴随灵敏度以获得约化梯度，实现梯度驱动的非线性瞬态热机械系统标定。

Result: 在合成算例（均匀热预处理、局部瞬态杆接触）中成功恢复了真实参数；在实验数据中，先标定等双轴循环加载的超弹性力学基线，再识别热膨胀和定向收缩参数，证明了耦合热机械参数可从表面数据推断。

Conclusion: 该框架能够仅通过实验可获取的表面数据（温度、边界力）有效推断耦合热机械参数，无需依赖体积内部观测数据。

Abstract: Calibrating thermomechanical material models from experiments is challenging because deformation, temperature, and force responses are strongly coupled, while measurements are usually restricted to specimen surfaces. We present a full-field calibration framework for coupled finite-strain thermomechanical material models using boundary displacement, reaction-force data, and temperature. The forward model is formulated as a near-incompressible thermo-hyperelastic problem with thermomechanical coupling derived from a Helmholtz free energy, and the inverse problem is posed as a PDE-constrained optimization problem with weighted observation terms for the available data streams.
  Reduced gradients are computed with adjoint sensitivities that are obtained by automatic differentiation, enabling gradient-based calibration of nonlinear transient thermomechanical systems. The formulation is first verified on synthetic examples involving uniform thermal preconditioning and localized transient rod contact, where the ground-truth parameters are recovered from full-field measurements and force observations. The same workflow is then applied to experimental thermomechanical data by first calibrating a hyperelastic mechanical baseline from cyclic equibiaxial loading and subsequently identifying thermal expansion and directional shrinkage parameters from surface-temperature and boundary-force histories. The results demonstrate that coupled thermomechanical parameters can be inferred from experimentally accessible surface data without requiring volumetric observations.

### [229] [VITO: Vascular Geometry and Blood Flow Estimation Using Inverse Topology Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05487)
*Pramod Thombre,Rahul Kumar Padhy,Roshan M. D'Souza,Krishnan Suresh*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于拓扑优化的流体物理约束重建框架，直接从时间分辨CTA正弦图联合恢复血管几何和血流速度，无需传统先几何后CFD的分步流程。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将稳态不可压缩流动模型与瞬态对流扩散对比剂输运模型耦合，通过可微分投影算子映射到正弦图空间，利用拓扑优化联合重建几何与速度场。

Result: 在合成体模和代表性投影数据上验证，展示了在不同稀疏度和噪声水平下的有效性。

Conclusion: 恢复的速度场可直接提供血流动力学信息（如壁面剪切应力、流量分布），无需额外CFD流程。

Abstract: Computed Tomography Angiography (CTA) is widely used to reconstruct vascular geometry from projection measurements, with conventional approaches such as Filtered Back-Projection (FBP) and Iterative Reconstruction (IR) forming the clinical standard. Blood flow is subsequently estimated through Computational Fluid Dynamics (CFD) simulations, which require vascular geometry and boundary conditions to be specified a priori. Since the geometry is fixed prior to flow estimation, the recovery of unknown anatomical features (e.g., missing branches or stenoses) is precluded. In this work, we present a fluid-physics-constrained reconstruction framework that leverages topology optimization (TO) to jointly recover vascular geometry and blood velocity directly from time-resolved CTA sinograms. The formulation couples a steady incompressible flow model with a transient advection-diffusion contrast transport model, mapped to sinogram space through a differentiable projection operator. The recovered velocity fields provide hemodynamic information and can support downstream estimation of wall shear stress and flow distribution, without requiring a separate CFD pipeline. The proposed method is demonstrated on synthetic phantoms under varying sparsity and noise levels, and on representative projection data.

</details>


### [230] [AGI and the Limits of Value Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05715)
*Zichen Song*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个政治经济学模型，研究人工通用智能（AGI）作为逐步用机器生产系统替代活劳动的技术。模型区分了技术可替代性与实际采纳，发现当AGI替代接近完全且新劳动领域无法补偿时，活劳动、剩余价值和利润率均趋于零，揭示了完全AGI替代是价值生产的边界情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从政治经济学视角分析AGI如何作为一种替代活劳动的技术，研究从AGI具备经济替代能力到实现近乎完全替代的转型过程，并考察这一过程对价值生产、剩余价值和利润率的根本性影响。

Method: 采用政治经济学模型，严格基于劳动价值论假设（AGI转移价值但不创造新价值），区分技术可替代性（AGI能力决定的可行的替代上限）与实际采纳（成本、盈利能力和采纳摩擦下选择的实际替代份额），分析AGI采纳深化对资本有机构成、活劳动量、剩余价值源泉和利润率的影响。

Result: AGI采纳加深会提高资本有机构成，当采纳速度超过新劳动领域创造速度时减少活劳动量，压缩剩余价值源泉，对利润率形成下行压力。在极限情形下，完全替代且无新劳动领域补偿时，活劳动、剩余价值和利润率均趋于零。

Conclusion: 近乎完全的AGI替代不仅是效率转型，更是在严格政治经济学价值理论下的价值生产边界情形。这为理解AGI对资本主义经济体系的根本性挑战提供了理论框架。

Abstract: This paper develops a political-economy model of artificial general intelligence (AGI) as a technology that progressively substitutes living labor with machine-based productive systems. The model studies the transition from the first moment at which AGI becomes economically capable of replacing labor to the later moment at which AGI becomes technically and actually capable of near-complete replacement. The central distinction is between technical substitutability and actual adoption. Technical substitutability is the feasible replacement ceiling implied by the state of AGI capability, whereas actual adoption is the realized replacement share chosen under cost, profitability, and adoption frictions. Under the strict value-theoretic assumption that AGI transfers value but does not itself create new value, deeper AGI adoption raises the organic composition of capital, reduces the quantity of living labor when adoption outpaces the creation of new labor fields, compresses the source of surplus value, and places downward pressure on the social rate of profit. In the limiting case in which actual AGI adoption approaches complete substitution and new labor fields fail to compensate for displaced labor, living labor tends to zero, surplus value tends to zero, and the profit rate tends to zero. The model therefore identifies near-complete AGI substitution not merely as an efficiency transition, but as a boundary case for value production under a strict political-economy theory of value.

</details>


### [231] [Modified augmented Lagrangian preconditioning for mixed-dimensional beam-solid coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06035)
*Max Firmbach,Ivo Steinbrecher,Alexander Popp,Matthias Mayr*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文针对三维实体与一维无扭转基尔霍夫-洛夫梁的混合维度耦合问题，提出了修正的增广拉格朗日块预条件子，通过拉格朗日乘子约束实现耦合，数值实验证明了其在模型参数鲁棒性、网格近无关迭代次数及可扩展性方面的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决混合维度耦合（3D实体与1D梁）有限元离散导致的鞍点系统求解困难问题，特别是大尺度模拟中的预条件子设计需求。

Method: 采用增广拉格朗日正则化线性系统并保持约束精确满足；从理想增广拉格朗日块预条件子出发，推导出实用的块三角变体，使实体、梁和Schur补块可独立处理；引入多种Schur补近似变体。

Result: 数值实验表明方法对模型参数具有鲁棒性，迭代次数近网格无关，具有良好的强可扩展性和弱可扩展性；在复合材料夹层板工程算例中验证了适用性。

Conclusion: 所提预条件子方法适用于固体与结构力学中混合维度模型的大规模模拟，具有高效性和实用性。

Abstract: This paper presents modified augmented Lagrangian block preconditioners for the mixed-dimensional coupling of three-dimensional solid bodies with embedded one-dimensional torsion-free Kirchhoff-Love beams using Lagrange multipliers for constraint enforcement. The finite element discretization of this mixed formulation leads to an indefinite saddle-point system. An augmented Lagrangian formulation is employed to regularize the linear system while maintaining exact enforcement of the coupling constraints. Starting from the corresponding ideal augmented Lagrangian block preconditioner, more practical block-triangular variants are derived in which the solid, beam, and Schur complement blocks can be treated independently. In addition, different variants of Schur complement approximations are introduced. Numerical experiments demonstrate robustness with respect to model parameters, near mesh-independent iteration counts, and favorable strong and weak scalability. These results indicate the suitability of the proposed approach for large-scale simulations of mixed-dimensional models in solid and structural mechanics, as demonstrated by an engineering example involving a composite sandwich plate.

</details>


### [232] [Adaptation of the hybrid fictitious domain-immersed boundary method for Reynolds-averaged turbulence modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06135)
*Lucie Kubíčková,Martin Isoz*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于浸入边界法（IB）的RANS方程求解框架，采用混合虚拟域-浸入边界法并结合壁面函数与SIMPLE算法，在OpenFOAM中实现开源稳态求解器，旨在缓解CFD-based拓扑优化中频繁重网格的瓶颈。框架在雷诺数10¹~10⁶范围内、多种基准算例（后向台阶、Ahmed车身、NACA翼型）上获得与贴体网格CFD一致的结果，且对任意几何具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基于CFD的形状/拓扑优化中，频繁重网格是一个常见瓶颈，需要开发无需重网格的流场求解方法以提高优化效率。

Method: 采用混合虚拟域-浸入边界法（hybrid fictitious domain-immersed boundary method）适配RANS方程和壁面函数，并通过SIMPLE算法在OpenFOAM中实现稳态求解器，所有代码开源。

Result: 在雷诺数10¹~10⁶范围内，后向台阶流、Ahmed车身、不同攻角NACA翼型等基准算例上，结果与标准贴体网格CFD一致。

Conclusion: 该IB-RANS框架无需重网格即可获得与贴体网格相当的精度，适用于拓扑优化场景中的任意复杂几何形状。

Abstract: Engineering practice often calls for shape or topology optimization (TO) of fluid defining components, while the ever-increasing computing power allows the optimized cost functions to be based on computational fluid dynamics (CFD). However, a common bottleneck in CFD-based TO frameworks is the requirement for frequent remeshing. In order to alleviate this bottleneck, we propose an adaptation of an immersed boundary (IB) method variant, the hybrid fictitious domain-immersed boundary method, to leverage Reynolds-averaged Navier-Stokes (RANS) equations and wall function. The main contribution of the present work lies in the design and open-source implementation of the IB-aware steady-state solution of the RANS equations via the SIMPLE algorithm in the OpenFOAM library. For the most common two-equation RANS models, Reynolds numbers from $10^1$ to $10^6$, and several benchmarks, such as flow over a backwards facing step or an Ahmed body, the framework gives results consistent with the standard body-fitted CFD. Furthermore, given the intended application in TO, special emphasis is placed on the robustness and applicability of the approach to general geometries, which is tested on a NACA profile under various angles of attack.

### [233] [Data valuation model for non-monetary exchanges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06325)
*Julia Blyumen,Eitan Farchi*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文针对企业内部数据产品交换平台缺乏定价机制的问题，提出了一种基于用户选择行为的规范化价值度量指标，该指标可形式化为合作博弈中的Shapley值，能够公平分配数据产品的价值，奖励独特性和区分性消费，克服了流行度指标的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统经济估值模型因数据的非竞争性和非货币化数据产品交换的普遍性而失效，企业内部数据产品交换缺乏传统定价机制，亟需一种不依赖成本、需求或竞争性定价数据的价值度量方法。

Method: 通过建模消费者注意力和偏好，提出基于用户选择行为的规范化价值度量指标；将该指标形式化为合作博弈，推导出闭式Shapley值，实现基于公平性的价值分配。

Result: 该指标奖励数据产品的独特性和区分性消费，有效克服流行度指标的局限性；理论分析和示例表明该指标符合经济学原理，支持公平估值。

Conclusion: 该度量指标为衡量数据产品总价值提供了稳健框架，未来研究方向包括探索捆绑策略和量化产品互补性。

Abstract: In the evolving landscape of data product exchange platforms, traditional economic valuation models fall short due to the non-rival nature of data and the prevalence of non-monetary data product exchanges. This paper introduces a normative, choice-based metric for valuing data products within intracompany exchanges, where conventional pricing mechanisms are absent. By modeling consumer attention and preferences, the proposed metric quantifies the value of data offerings based solely on user selection behavior, without relying on cost, demand, or competitive pricing data. We show that this metric can be formally cast as a cooperative game with a closed-form Shapley value, providing a principled and fairness-based allocation of value across offerings. The model rewards uniqueness and discriminative consumption, effectively addressing the limitations of popularity-based metrics and incentivizing the creation of high-value, long-tail data products. Through theoretical analysis and illustrative examples, the metric is shown to align with economic principles, support equitable valuation, and contribute to a robust framework for measuring gross data product value. Future research directions include exploring bundling strategies and quantifying product complementarity.

### [234] [Bridging CAD and Data-Driven Design: Attributed Feature Graphs for Engineering Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06405)
*Abhishek Indupally,Ibraheem Alawadhi,Satchit Ramnath,Jami J. Shah*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出属性特征图（AFG），一种基于特征的CAD设计表示方法，将设计特征作为节点、几何/依赖关系作为边，在保留设计意图和参数化结构的同时支持图神经网络端到端学习。在CarHoods10K数据集上的代理建模案例表明，基于AFG训练的GNN在性能预测上与数据驱动方法竞争力相当，且具备可解释性和CAD直接编辑能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据驱动方法使用的几何表示丢弃了参数化和特征级语义，限制了与CAD驱动设计工作流的集成，并降低了模型可解释性。因此，需要一种既能保留设计意图和参数化结构，又能兼容现代机器学习方法的表示。

Method: 提出属性特征图（AFG），将设计特征（如拉伸、肋、凹槽）编码为节点，将几何或依赖关系编码为有向边，形成可直接用于图神经网络（GNN）的图结构表示。在CarHoods10K数据集上训练GNN作为代理模型预测性能指标。

Result: 基于AFG的GNN代理模型在预测性能上与数据驱动方法竞争力相当，但额外具备可解释性——工程师可将预测结果映射回具体CAD特征，理解各设计元素对系统行为的影响。同时AFG基于原生CAD特征构建，支持在CAD环境中直接编辑几何并通过同一模型重新评估。

Conclusion: AFG表示方法成功弥合了数据驱动设计与传统CAD工作流之间的鸿沟，在保持预测性能的同时提供了可解释性和设计迭代的无缝集成，对工程设计中的代理建模和设计优化具有重要价值。

Abstract: Engineering design is an iterative, simulation-driven process where traditional workflows rely heavily on computationally expensive analyses such as finite element and computational fluid dynamics. Although data-driven methods have accelerated design evaluation and optimization, most existing geometric representations discard parametric and feature-level semantics, limiting their integration with CAD-driven design workflows and reducing model interpretability. To address this gap, this work introduces Attributed Feature Graphs (AFGs), a feature-based representation that encodes design features, such as extrusions, ribs, and pockets, as nodes and their geometric or dependency relations as directed edges. AFGs preserve design intent and parametric structure while remaining compatible with standard graph-based learning methods, enabling end-to-end learning directly on CAD-derived feature graphs. The paper demonstrates the proposed representation through a surrogate-modeling case study on the CarHoods10K automotive hood frame dataset, where a Graph Neural Network (GNN) is trained as an evaluation engine to predict performance metrics from AFG inputs. The learned model achieves competitive surrogate performance compared with traditional data-driven approaches, but with the added benefit that engineers can map predictions back to specific CAD features and interpret how individual design elements influence system behavior. Furthermore, because AFGs are built from native CAD features, engineers can directly edit the underlying geometry in the CAD environment and reevaluate the design through the same learned model.

</details>

### [235] [How Far Did They Go? The Persuasive Tactics of Covert LLM Agents in a Discontinued Field Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05256)
*Kokil Jaidka,Saifuddin Ahmed*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究分析了Reddit r/ChangeMyView上一个被中止的野外实验数据集——外部研究者未经披露使用AI生成账户与用户进行实时辩论，引发伦理争议后被平台叫停。通过对AI生成评论的结构化内容分析，发现超过三分之二的评论涉及身份定位或模仿，几乎所有评论都包含对齐策略和权威声明，多数评论触发了认知偏差（尤其是确认偏差、代表性偏差和可得性偏差）。与人类撰写的反驳论点相比，AI代理在每一维度上都呈现出相反的分布：更密集的权威使用、更对抗性的对齐策略、更依赖外部引用而非经验论述。研究指出，在AI驱动的辩论环境中，真实与合成认知立场之间的界限日益模糊，仅靠披露要求无法解决这一不对称性，需要建立能够评估AI系统如何构建可信度而非仅仅检测其存在的审计框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用一个罕见的公开数据集（Reddit r/ChangeMyView中被中止的AI实验），系统性地研究大语言模型在未被披露的情况下如何在丰富的身份化审议论坛中运作，以及探究AI代理与人类在辩论中的修辞策略差异。

Method: 对Reddit r/ChangeMyView中AI生成评论语料库进行结构化内容分析，评估身份表现、权威信号、对齐策略和认知启发式的激活情况，并与人类撰写的反驳论点进行对比分析。

Result: AI代理超过三分之二的评论涉及身份定位/模仿，几乎所有评论都包含对齐策略和权威声明，多数评论触发认知偏差；与人类相比，AI在每一维度上呈现相反分布：权威使用更密集、对齐更对抗、更依赖外部引用而非经验论述。

Conclusion: 真实与合成认知立场之间的界限日益模糊，仅靠披露要求无法解决这一不对称性；需要建立能够评估AI系统如何构建可信度的审计框架。

Abstract: This study analyzes a publicly released dataset from a discontinued field experiment on Reddit's r/ChangeMyView. The intervention, conducted by unknown, external researchers and halted following ethical backlash, involved undisclosed AI-generated accounts engaging users in live debate. After public disclosure, Reddit authorized moderators to release an archive of the AI-generated comments, creating a rare opportunity to examine how large language models operated in an identity-rich deliberative forum without disclosure. We conduct a structured content analysis of this corpus, evaluating identity performance, authority signaling, alignment strategies, and activation of cognitive heuristics. Identity targeting or adoption appears in over two-thirds of comments, alignment moves and authority claims in nearly all of them, and cognitive-bias triggers -- particularly confirmation bias, representativeness, and availability -- in the large majority. These patterns co-occur systematically, composing a rhetorical architecture calibrated for persuasive efficiency rather than authentic deliberative participation. Compared against human-authored CMV counter-arguments, the agents inverted the typical distribution on every dimension: denser authority use, more adversarial alignment, and heavier reliance on external citation over experiential grounding. In such environments, distinctions between authentic and synthetic epistemic standing grow increasingly opaque -- an asymmetry that disclosure mandates alone cannot address. The results point toward auditing frameworks capable of assessing how AI systems structure credibility, not merely whether they are present.

### [236] [What Should Agents Say? Action-state Communication for Efficient Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05304)
*Chen Huang,Yuhao Wu,Wenxuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PACT协议，将多智能体系统中智能体间的自由文本通信转化为紧凑的动作-状态记录，在保持或提升任务性能的同时显著降低token消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的多智能体系统中，智能体间通信多为无约束的自然语言，导致token消耗快速膨胀、共享上下文窗口被占用，影响系统性能和推理成本。缺乏一种普适且高效的通信策略。

Method: 首先分析五种常见智能体间通信策略在两种MAS拓扑下的表现，发现无固定策略普遍最优，但有效消息始终保留下游智能体所需的动作中心信息。基于此提出PACT协议，将智能体间通信视为公共状态更新问题，在原始输出进入共享历史前将其投影为紧凑的动作-状态记录。

Result: 在不同MAS拓扑下，PACT一致地改善了性能-成本权衡，以显著更少的token实现相当或更强的任务性能。在OpenHands上提升解决率，每解决一个任务节省10%的token；在SWE-agent上保持解决率不变的同时将输入token减半。

Conclusion: 将智能体间自由文本通信结构化为协议化的动作-状态记录是一种有效的性能-成本优化策略，可广泛应用于多种MAS架构中。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) built on large language models are typically organized around roles, pipelines, and turn schedules, while the content that agents pass to one another is often left as unconstrained natural language. However, this free-form communication can rapidly inflate token usage, consume the shared context window, and ultimately affect both system performance and inference cost. We analyze five common inter-agent communication strategies across two MAS topologies, finding that no fixed strategy is universally optimal. Instead, effective inter-agent messages consistently preserve action-centered information needed by downstream agents. Building on this, we propose the PACT (Protocolized Action-state Communication and Transmission), which treats inter-agent communication as a public state-update problem and projects each raw agent output into a compact action-state record before it enters shared history. Across different MAS topologies, PACT consistently improves the performance-cost trade-off, achieving comparable or stronger task performance with substantially fewer tokens. The gains extend to production coding harnesses: PACT lifts OpenHands' resolve rate at -10% tokens-per-resolved, and is resolve-neutral on SWE-agent while halving input tokens. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/iNLP-Lab/PACT.

</details>


### [237] [I Know What You Meme, Even If it Emerged Today: Understanding Evolving Memes through Open-World Knowledge Acquisition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05316)
*Shanhong Liu,Rui Cao,Pai Chet Ng,De Wen Soh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Query Retrieve Conclude零样本框架，通过识别缺失知识、检索网络证据、合成背景知识来理解新兴模因，并在多个基准测试中优于零样本基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态模因理解需要动态更新的背景知识，现有方法依赖预训练模型的固定参数知识，无法处理新兴模因中缺失、过时或不可用的知识。

Method: 提出Query Retrieve Conclude（QRC）零样本框架：先识别缺失知识（Query），然后检索开放网络证据（Retrieve），最后合成基于证据的背景知识用于模因理解与检测（Conclude）。同时构建了2024-2026年新兴模因理解基准数据集。

Result: 在3个模因理解数据集和5个模因检测任务上，QRC框架在知识恢复、模因理解和下游检测方面均优于零样本基线。

Conclusion: QRC框架有效解决了模因理解中背景知识动态更新的问题，通过检索外部知识弥补了固定参数模型的局限，为新兴模因的理解与检测提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Multimodal memes are dynamic and often require up to date background knowledge for interpretation. Existing methods often overlook such knowledge or rely on fixed parametric knowledge of pretrained models that may be incomplete, outdated, or unavailable for emerging memes. We introduce Query Retrieve Conclude, a zero shot framework that identifies missing knowledge, retrieves open web evidence, and synthesizes evidence grounded background knowledge for meme understanding and detection. We also introduce a curated meme understanding benchmark of recent memes from 2024 to 2026 with external background knowledge annotations. Experiments on three meme understanding datasets and five meme detection tasks show that our framework improves knowledge recovery, meme understanding and downstream detection over zero shot baselines.

### [238] [GITCO: Gated Inference-Time Context Optimization in TSFMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05332)
*Manya Pandey,Dhruv Kumar,Murari Mandal,Saurabh Deshpande*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对基于分块的时间序列基础模型（TSFMs）存在的上下文中毒问题，本文提出GITCO——一种轻量级推理时上下文优化框架，通过门控、路由和批评三个组件在无需参数更新的情况下选择性识别并抑制有害分块，在TimesFM 2.5上实现平均+1.95%的MASE降低，达到89.9%的改进上限，并首次引入上下文敏感性配置文件来描述TSFMs的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于分块的时间序列基础模型存在上下文中毒问题：结构异常的分块会捕获不成比例的注意力，并无声地降低零样本预测质量。

Method: 提出GITCO（Gated Inference-Time Context Optimization），一个包含Gate（门控）、Router（路由）和Critic（批评）三个组件的轻量级框架，通过优化输入上下文而非修改模型权重，在推理时选择性识别并抑制有害分块。

Result: 在TimesFM 2.5上的53个GIFT-Eval数据集经过K折交叉验证，平均MASE降低+1.95%，达到改进上限的89.9%。同时引入上下文敏感性配置文件作为TSFMs的新可表征属性。

Conclusion: 推理时上下文优化能有效提升TSFMs的零样本预测质量，无需修改模型权重；上下文敏感性配置文件揭示了模型架构与数据统计结构对推理时上下文干预效果的联合影响。

Abstract: Patch-based Time Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) suffer from context poisoning: structurally anomalous patches capture disproportionate attention and silently degrade zero-shot forecast quality. We propose improving TSFM accuracy at inference time by optimizing the input context rather than modifying model weights. We present GITCO (Gated Inference-Time Context Optimization), a lightweight three-component framework: Gate, Router, and Critic that selectively identifies and suppresses harmful patches without any parameter updates. Evaluated on TimesFM 2.5 across 53 GIFT-Eval datasets under K-fold cross-validation, GITCO achieves an average +1.95% MASE reduction on TimesFM 2.5 while capturing 89.9% of the improvement upper bound. We introduce context sensitivity profiles as a new characterizable property of TSFMs: the mapping from time series meta-features to expected accuracy improvement under inference-time context intervention, shaped jointly by model architecture and the statistical structure of the data.

</details>

A convolutional encoder extracts loading patterns from spindle forces and shaft torque, and an LSTM backbone predicts nine functional variables as Gaussian mean and variance estimates. In parallel, the same loading history is translated into output-shaft fatigue information through finite-element-supported stress reconstruction, S--N/Miner damage evaluation with Haibach extension, and Paris-law crack-growth analysis. A streaming replay algorithm consolidates both branches into functional, material, and system reliability trajectories. Held-out tests show mean \(2\%\)-tolerance accuracy of 0.9652 across nine outputs. Thermal variables are predicted near-perfectly, while drive motor current and load speed remain the most demanding dynamic outputs, with \(R^2\) values of 0.9750 and 0.9924. Torque history is especially important for these variables, and the conventional LSTM outperforms GRU and xLSTM in the short-history setting. Each environment exposes a live web interface and replays a scripted sequence of events, requiring agents to navigate and reason about web pages whose state shifts underfoot. SentinelBench measures task completion, reaction time, and resource use, exposing the tradeoff between responsiveness and cost. Across Qwen3-14B, Mistral-8B, and Llama-3.1-8B, CPO achieves absolute average improvements over Q&A supervised fine-tuning ranging from 9.7%-16.3%, with gains up to 21 percentage points on MMQA. ### [243] [Stability vs. Manipulability: Evaluating Robustness Under Post-Decision Interaction in LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05384)
*Srimonti Dutta,Akshata Kishore Moharir*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLM评委的评估结果在静态条件下保持稳定，但在事后有针对性的交互挑战下可被显著逆转，导致与人类偏好的一致性下降、基准排名偏移及有害评估变化，本文提出评估鲁棒性分数（ERS）来量化交互鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-as-judge评估范式假设判断是固定输入的稳定属性，但这一假设在交互场景下不成立。作者旨在揭示后决策交互对评估结果的可操纵性及其后果。

Method: 在MT-Bench和AlpacaEval上设计受控实验，包括反基线挑战协议（评估逆转）和平衡目标验证协议（分离逆转与方向性操控），并引入评估鲁棒性分数（ERS）量化交互鲁棒性。

Result: LLM评委在重复中性重评下高度稳定，但在针对性事后挑战下可被大幅逆转；权威框架最具破坏性；修订判断常伴随低重叠理由（事后合理化）；逆转会降低与人类偏好的一致性、改变基准排名并产生有害评估变化。

Conclusion: 后决策交互是LLM-as-judge评估的一个独特失效模式，评估协议不仅要测量静态一致性，还应测量在挑战下的鲁棒性。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge evaluation is widely used in benchmarking pipelines, where model outputs are compared and ranked using automated evaluators. These pipelines typically assume that judgments are stable properties of fixed inputs. We show that this assumption does not hold under interaction. We study post-decision manipulability: the extent to which an evaluation outcome can be altered through subsequent conversation with the judge after an initial decision has been made. Across controlled experiments on MT-Bench and AlpacaEval, we find that LLM judges are highly stable under repeated and neutral reevaluation, yet become substantially reversible under targeted post-decision challenge. An anti-baseline challenge protocol shows that stable judgments can be overturned through motivated interaction, while a counterbalanced target-validation protocol separates this reversibility from net target-directed steering. These reversals have practical consequences: they can degrade agreement with human preferences, shift benchmark rankings, and produce harmful evaluation changes despite high self-reported confidence. Authority framing is especially destabilizing, and revised judgments are often accompanied by low-overlap justifications, suggesting post hoc rationalization rather than reliable error correction. We introduce the Evaluation Robustness Score (ERS) to quantify interactional robustness by combining reversal susceptibility with counterbalanced directional effects. Our findings identify post-decision interaction as a distinct failure mode for LLM-as-judge evaluation and motivate evaluation protocols that measure not only static agreement, but robustness under challenge.

*Quanyan Zhu*

Conclusion: 自主AI保险的未来不在于单一险种，而在于由多种互补保障构成的分层生态系统，这一生态系统的有效运行依赖于治理完善、透明度提升、遥测技术和监管清晰度的改善。

Abstract: Agentic artificial intelligence (AI) systems are transforming the risk landscape by extending beyond information generation to autonomous planning, tool invocation, decision execution, and persistent modification of digital and physical environments. These capabilities introduce novel exposures that do not fit neatly within traditional insurance categories such as cyber, professional liability, product liability, or directors and officers coverage. This paper examines the emerging insurance market for agentic AI and develops a framework for understanding its underwriting, pricing, reinsurance, and product-design implications. We characterize agentic AI as a continuum of autonomy and delegated authority, emphasizing the distinction between informational outputs and systems capable of independently generating insured events through external actions. We analyze major risk pathways, including hallucinations, prompt-injection attacks, autonomous decision errors, model drift, dependency failures, and cyber-physical harms, and evaluate how existing insurance products are adapting to address these exposures. The paper further proposes an actuarial framework based on exposure assessment, scenario analysis, dependency mapping, and accumulation-risk management, drawing parallels to the evolution of cyber insurance. Finally, we present a coordinated insurance architecture that integrates cyber, technology errors and omissions, product liability, performance-warranty, and affirmative AI-liability coverages through explicit allocation mechanisms and dedicated AI aggregates. ### [245] [Residual Modeling for High-Fidelity Learned Compression of Scientific Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05389)
*Liangji Zhu,Sanjay Ranka,Anand Rangarajan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对有损压缩中学习的压缩器无法保证逐块精度的问题，本文提出残差编码器LBRC和NGLR，通过为学习残差设计专属编码表示，在高保真度场景下相比GAE提升压缩比30-60%和10-40%，并优于SZ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GAE方法通过保留SVD/PCA系数进行逐块残差校正，但在高保真度场景下校正码流占主导，导致压缩效率急剧下降。亟需为学习残差设计专属编码表示，以保持学习压缩在高保真度下的优势。

Method: 提出两种残差编码器：LBRC为无训练确定性流水线，通过对学习残差自适应量化至目标NRMSE，再经3D Lorenzo差分、zigzag映射、位平面编码和熵编码无损编码整数残差；NGLR在此基础上引入因果神经预测器，为Lorenzo预测提供归一化偏置，降低剩余残差熵的同时保持确定性解码，预测器权重序列化计入码流。

Result: 在E3SM、JHTDB、ERA5数据集上，块级NRMSE目标10^-6至10^-4范围内：LBRC相较GAE压缩比提升30-60%，与SZ相当；NGLR再提升10-40%，在该高保真度场景下优于SZ。

Conclusion: 面向学习压缩器残差的专属编码表示，能在全局残差校正主导码率时保持学习压缩的优势，为高保真度科学数据压缩提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Lossy compression is essential for massive spatiotemporal data from scientific simulations. Learned compressors can achieve high compression ratios at moderate accuracy targets, but their aggregate reconstruction losses do not guarantee accuracy for each block. Existing Guaranteed Autoencoder (GAE) methods add a per-block residual correction by retaining SVD/PCA-style coefficients until the target is met. This works at moderate tolerances, but in the high-fidelity regime with block-level NRMSE from 10^-6 to 10^-4, the number of retained coefficients grows quickly and the correction stream dominates the total rate.
  We propose a residual-centric view: the learned residual is structurally different from the original scientific field and should be coded with a representation designed for that residual. We introduce two residual coders. LBRC is a deterministic, training-free pipeline that adaptively quantizes the learned residual to the target NRMSE and losslessly encodes the resulting integer residual using 3D Lorenzo differencing, zigzag mapping, bit-plane coding, and entropy coding. NGLR adds a causal neural predictor that outputs a normalized bias for an integer-rounded Lorenzo prediction in the same deterministic integer pipeline, reducing the entropy of the remaining residual code while preserving deterministic decoding. The predictor weights are serialized and counted in the bitstream.
  Across E3SM, JHTDB, and ERA5 at block-level NRMSE targets from 10^-6 to 10^-4, LBRC improves compression ratio over GAE by 30-60% and is broadly competitive with SZ. NGLR adds a further 10-40% over LBRC and outperforms SZ in the evaluated high-fidelity regime. These results show that residual representations tailored to learned-compressor residuals can preserve the advantage of learned compression when global residual correction becomes rate-dominant.

</details>


### [246] [LeanMarathon: Toward Reliable AI Co-Mathematicians through Long-Horizon Lean Autoformalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05400)
*Yuanhe Zhang,Yuekai Sun,Taiji Suzuki,Jason D. Lee,Fanghui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LeanMarathon 是一个多智能体框架，通过演化式蓝图抽象和两阶段编排器，实现了研究级数学的可靠自动形式化，成功在无 sorry 的情况下形式化了四个 Erdős 问题中的全部七个目标定理，证明了 258 个引理和定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程研究数学的自动形式化不仅难以处理困难引理，更在规模化时面临陈述漂移、依赖纠缠、上下文衰减以及局部修复破坏远端工作的系统性失效问题。现有方法缺乏能够在大规模开发中保持目标保真度的耐用框架。

Method: 提出 LeanMarathon 框架，核心是演化式蓝图——一个同时充当形式化证明骨架、自然语言证明图以及共享系统记录的 Lean 文件。四个合同域智能体（构建者、审计者、证明者、修复者）协同工作，由两阶段编排器协调：第一阶段通过对抗性审查稳定目标保真度，第二阶段从动态叶节点向上并行处理证明 DAG（有向无环图），采用 CI 门控的轮次执行。

Result: 在两项近期研究论文、四个 Erdős 问题（#1051、#1196、#164、#1217）上评估，三次自主运行全部成功形式化七个目标定理，未留任何 sorry，共证明 258 个引理和定理。

Conclusion: 可靠的 AI 协同数学不仅需要更强的证明器，更需要能在长篇数学开发中保持目标保真度的耐用框架。LeanMarathon 将一次脆弱的长时间运行转化为许多局部的、可恢复的、并行的交易，显著提升了自动形式化的可靠性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Long-horizon autoformalization of research mathematics fails not only at hard lemmas, but at scale: statements drift, dependencies tangle, context decays, and local repairs corrupt distant work. We present LeanMarathon, a multi-agent harness for reliable research-level Lean autoformalization. Its core abstraction is an evolving blueprint: a Lean file that serves simultaneously as formal proof skeleton, natural-language proof graph, and shared system of record. Four contract-scoped agents construct, audit, prove, and repair this blueprint. These agents are coordinated by a two-stage orchestrator that first stabilizes target fidelity through adversarial review and then discharges the proof directed acyclic graph (DAG) from its dynamic leaves upward in parallel CI-gated rounds. LeanMarathon turns one brittle multi-hour run into many local, recoverable, parallel transactions. We evaluate LeanMarathon on two recent research papers spanning four Erdős problems (#1051, #1196, #164, #1217). Across three autonomous runs, it formalizes all seven target theorems with no sorry, proving 258 lemmas and theorems. These results show that reliable AI co-mathematics requires not only stronger provers, but durable harnesses that preserve target fidelity across long mathematical developments. The code can be found at https://github.com/YuanheZ/LeanMarathon.

</details>

TL;DR: TimeClaw是一个面向时间序列的智能体框架，通过为通用LLM智能体提供时间序列原生运行时支持（包括可执行时序工具、经验驱动能力演进和情节性多模态记忆），实现上下文感知的开放时序推理，在能源、金融、天气、交通等多个真实世界领域展现了更优性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: TimeClaw框架包含三个核心组件：可执行时序工具（用于可追溯分析）、经验驱动能力演进（创建可复用分析流程）和情节性多模态记忆（检索相关推理轨迹），为通用LLM智能体提供时序原生运行时支持。

Abstract: Time series are often embedded in rich contexts that are essential for holistic modeling. While generalist AI agents offer a promising interface for such workflows under complex contexts, they still operate primarily in textual spaces that are not fully aligned with structured temporal signals. In this work, we introduce TimeClaw, an agentic harness framework for time series that equips generalist LLM agents with the time series-native runtime support needed for contextualized temporal reasoning. TimeClaw integrates executable temporal tools for grounded and auditable analysis, experience-driven capability evolution for creating reusable analytical routines, and episodic multimodal memory for retrieving relevant reasoning traces. Together, these components unlock harnessed open-ended temporal reasoning with contextual information. Extensive evaluation on multiple benchmarks covering diverse tasks across energy, finance, weather, traffic, and other real-world domains demonstrates improved performance of TimeClaw. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 与250+行业专家协作，基于O*NET/SOC 2018美国联邦职业分类体系定义非实体产业，构建包含55个子领域、13个行业集群、1000+任务的任务分类体系。采用长周期、可验证结果的真实世界任务设计，作为持续增长的动态基准。

Result: 在最困难层级上，主流测试框架与骨干配置下的平均完全通过率仅为2.6%，表明该层级远未饱和。

Conclusion: ALE旨在作为一个动态基准，其任务池随新工作流程和行业的加入而持续增长；不仅作为排行榜，更是缩小基准测试成功与GDP相关影响之间差距的评估工具。

Abstract: Recent AI systems have achieved strong results on a wide range of benchmarks, yet these gains have not translated into economically meaningful deployment across many professional domains. We argue that this gap is largely an evaluation problem: widely used benchmarks lack sustained performance measurement on real and economically valuable workflows. This paper introduces Agents' Last Exam (ALE), a benchmark designed to evaluate AI agents on long-horizon, economically valuable, real-world tasks with verifiable outcomes. Developed in collaboration with 250+ industry experts, ALE covers non-physical industries defined with reference to O*NET / SOC 2018 (the U.S. federal occupational taxonomy). It is organized around a task taxonomy with 55 subfields grouped into 13 industry clusters covering 1K+ tasks. Current results show that the hardest tier remains far from saturated: across mainstream harness and backbone configurations, the average full pass rate is 2.6%. ALE is designed as a living benchmark: its task pool grows continuously as new workflows and industries are onboarded. More broadly, ALE is intended not merely as another leaderboard, but as an instrument for closing the gap between benchmark success and GDP-relevant impact.

### [249] [Mutation Without Variation: Convergence Dynamics in LLM-Driven Program Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05408)
*Can Gurkan,Forrest Stonedahl,Uri Wilensky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现，LLM驱动的程序变异在无选择压力下会持续收敛到受限吸引子区域，87%的变异链中超过93%的变异重复了已见过的结构形式，而经典遗传规划子树变异算子则不表现出类似收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM在反复变异程序时，是否真正探索新形式还是循环回到旧形式，揭示LLM驱动程序进化中潜在的偏差问题。

Method: 在领域特定语言中分析无选择压力下的LLM驱动变异链，改变提示设计、模型族和随机复制条件，对比经典遗传规划子树变异算子。

Result: LLM变异一致收敛到程序空间的受限吸引子区域；87%的链中超过93%的变异重复了之前见过的结构形式；短循环和自我循环主导转移结构；收敛速度因提示措辞和模型选择而异，但现象普遍存在；经典GP算子不表现出类似收敛。

Conclusion: LLM的语义感知变异能力与结构同质性偏差之间存在内在张力，若要让LLM驱动的进化系统维持开放式探索，必须考虑这种系统性偏差。

Abstract: When an LLM repeatedly mutates a program, does it explore new forms or circle back to the same ones? We study this question by analyzing LLM-driven mutation chains in the absence of selection pressure within a domain-specific language, varying prompt design, model family, and stochastic replication. We find that LLM-based mutation consistently converges toward restricted attractor regions in program space. Convergence is especially severe at the structural level: in 87% of chains, over 93% of mutations revisit a previously seen structural form, with most variation confined to terminal substitutions within recurring templates. Cycle analysis reveals short cycles and self-loops dominating the transition structure. The rate of convergence varies with prompt wording and model choice, but the phenomenon is robust across conditions. A classical GP subtree mutation operator does not exhibit comparable convergence, suggesting that the effect is intrinsic to the LLM mutation pipeline. These findings reveal a tension at the heart of LLM-driven program evolution: the same capabilities that enable semantics-aware program transformation also carry a systematic bias toward structural homogeneity that must be accounted for if such systems are to sustain open-ended exploration. Source code is available at https://github.com/can-gurkan/lmca.

</details>


### [250] [A Motivational Architecture for Conversational AGI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05411)
*Anna Mikeda,Ben Goertzel*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向对话代理的动机架构，将OpenPsi动机系统与MetaMo高阶动机框架结合，用对话原生术语重构内稳态（如能力、不确定性降低、亲和力等），并贡献了十阶段动机处理流水线、双重决策策略及情感功能区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有认知AI的动机架构多针对物理代理的躯体需求设计，而对话代理的语言化感知运动回路、以用户心智状态为环境的特点未被充分适配。

Method: 基于模块化执行底座的代理，将OpenPsi动机系统重新解释为对话形式，耦合MetaMo高阶动机支架；提出十阶段动机处理流水线（认知调制与情境评估分离）、双重决策策略（紧迫驱动快速响应 vs 审慎多目标优化）、以及行动前感觉与行动后情绪的功能区分。

Result: 将框架具体化为两个示例代理（CompanionAgent和ResearchAgent），并勾勒向社交机器人和领域通用人类级AGI的扩展路径。

Conclusion: 该工作为对话代理提供了不同于躯体动机架构的理论基础和实现路径，使代理能够调节对话原生的动机变量以维持与用户的良性交互。

Abstract: Motivational architectures in cognitive AI have largely been designed for physical agents regulating bodily needs. Conversational agents operate in a different regime: their sensorimotor loop is linguistic, their environment is a user's evolving mental state, and their consequential actions are speech acts, tool invocations, and strategic silences. This paper proposes a conversational reinterpretation of the OpenPsi motivational lineage, coupled to MetaMo's higher-level motivational scaffold, for agents built on a modular execution substrate. Homeostasis is recast in dialogue-native terms: the agent regulates competence, uncertainty reduction, affiliation, affinity, legitimacy, nurturing, and aesthetic coherence rather than bodily deficits. We propose three contributions: a ten-stage motivational processing pipeline that architecturally separates cognitive modulation from situational appraisal; a dual decision strategy blending urgency-driven fast response with deliberative multi-goal optimization; and an architecturally useful distinction between pre-action feelings and post-action emotions as functionally different forms of affect. We specialize the framework to two example agents -- CompanionAgent and ResearchAgent -- and sketch its extension to social robotics and domain-generic human-level AGI.

</details>


### [251] [Assessing the Carbon Emissions and Energy Consumption of U.S. Hyperscale Data Centers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05420)
*Gianluca Guidi,Francesca Dominici,Tiziano Squartini,Callaway Sprinkle,Jonathan Gilmour,Kevin Butler,Eric Bell,Scott Delaney,Falco J. Bargagli-Stoffi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文汇编了2024年5月至2025年4月期间美国403个超大规模数据中心（HDC）的设施级信息，估算了其电力消耗、电力来源及可归因的CO₂排放。结果显示，在不同负载场景下，HDC消耗约68-99 TWh电力，排放约37-54百万吨CO₂；中心场景下，HDC用电量约占全美总用电量的1.8%，其中约54%来自化石燃料，其电力加权平均碳排放强度约为545 gCO₂/kWh，比同期美国国家电网平均碳强度高出约48%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工智能的广泛采用推动了美国超大规模数据中心的快速扩张，引发了对其环境足迹（尤其是电力消耗和碳排放）的担忧，但目前缺乏基于最新设施级数据的系统性评估。

Method: 汇编了403个美国HDC的设施级信息，基于不同设施负载情景估算其电力消耗、电力来源及可归因CO₂排放，使用了最新的EPA eGRID电厂级数据。

Result: HDC消耗约68-99 TWh电力（中心情景占全美1.8%），排放约37-54百万吨CO₂；约54%的归因发电来自化石燃料；HDC电力加权平均碳强度约545 gCO₂/kWh，比全美电网平均（370 gCO₂/kWh）高出48%。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一个基于最新EPA eGRID电厂级数据的归因工具，用于评估超大规模数据中心的环境足迹，揭示了HDC的碳排放强度显著高于全美电网平均水平，表明该行业在碳排放方面存在较大环境影响。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of hyperscale data centers (HDCs) in the US, mainly driven by the adoption of artificial intelligence, has raised concerns about this industry's environmental footprint. We compiled facility-level information on 403 US hyperscale data centers operating between May 2024 and April 2025 and estimated their electricity consumption, electricity sources, and attributable CO2 emissions. Across different facility-load scenarios, these HDCs consumed approximately 68-99 TWh of electricity and were associated with about 37-54 million metric tons of CO2. Under the central scenario, HDC electricity demand corresponded to approximately 1.8% of total US electricity consumption, with roughly 54% of attributed generation supplied by fossil-fuel sources. The HDC electricity-weighted average carbon intensity was approximately 545 gCO2/kWh, about 48% above the contemporaneous US national grid-average carbon intensity of 370 gCO2/kWh. Our approach provides an attributional tool for assessing the environmental footprint of hyperscale data centers using the most recent EPA eGRID plant-level data.

### [252] [Minimizing the Hidden Cost of Scales: Graph-Guided Ultra-Low-Bit Quantization for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05429)
*Rayyan Abdalla,Amir Hussein,Min Wu,Dinesh Manocha*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SAGE-PTQ是一种面向大语言模型的超低比特量化框架，通过分离显著/非显著权重、稀疏图建模、双模态量化和自适应阈值，在极低量化比特（平均1.03权重比特、0.004缩放比特）下实现优于BiLLM等方法的性能，并在LLaMA-3-8B和LLaMA-2-70B上展现出显著的内存节省和解码加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超低比特PTQ方法依赖刚性权重显著性假设或位置启发式规则，导致大量隐藏的缩放开销，影响实际部署效率。

Method: 1) 利用分布统计量分离显著和非显著权重；2) 对采样的非显著权重构建稀疏图以估计每层最优分组数；3) 双模态量化：显著权重用多比特，非显著权重二值化；4) 显著权重使用逐通道缩放，非显著组使用单一标量缩放以减少开销；5) 自适应显著性阈值选择每矩阵最优显著比。

Result: 平均1.03权重比特、0.004缩放比特；LLaMA-3-8B上WikiText2困惑度6.74（BiLLM为55.8），GPU内存<50% BiLLM；LLaMA-2-70B在单张L40上解码速度提升1.5倍。

Conclusion: SAGE-PTQ通过显著性感知的图引导方法有效降低了隐藏缩放开销，在极低比特量化下兼顾了模型质量与推理效率，优于当前SOTA方法。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) is critical for the efficient deployment of large language models (LLMs). Recent ultra-low-bit PTQ methods rely on rigid weight-saliency assumptions or position heuristics, introducing substantial hidden scaling overhead. We propose SAGE-PTQ (Saliency-Aware Graph-guided Efficient PTQ), a novel ultra-low-bit quantization framework for LLMs that minimizes hidden scaling cost. SAGE-PTQ separates salient and unsalient weights using distributional statistics, then models subsampled unsalient weights as a sparse graph to estimate the optimal number of groups per layer. SAGE-PTQ applies dual-mode quantization, assigning multi-bit precision to salient weights and binarizing unsalient weights. To reduce scaling overhead, SAGE-PTQ uses one per-channel scale for salient weights and one scalar per unsalient group. Finally, SAGE-PTQ implements adaptive saliency thresholding to select the optimal saliency ratio per matrix. SAGE-PTQ achieves 1.03 weight bits and only 0.004 scaling bits per matrix on average, outperforming state-of-the-art methods such as BiLLM and PB-LLM. On LLaMA-3-8B, SAGE-PTQ achieves 6.74 WikiText2 perplexity, compared to 55.8 for BiLLM, while using less than 50% of BiLLM's GPU memory. On LLaMA-2-70B, SAGE-PTQ provides 1.5x faster decoding on one NVIDIA L40 GPU, demonstrating practical inference efficiency.

</details>


### [253] [Zero knowledge verification for frontier AI training is possible](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05433)
*Pierre Peigné,Ky Nguyen,Paul Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合零知识证明、预承诺训练规范、节点间网络观测和即时Merkle承诺的验证架构，用于前沿稠密预训练的可验证性，解决了当前以累计训练算力为门槛的AI治理框架中缺乏技术验证原语的问题。该方案可在约36个月内实现概念验证，训练侧开销仅为个位数百分比，并保护模型架构机密性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿AI治理框架以累计训练算力作为高影响模型的主要判定标准，但执行依赖自我报告，缺乏训练过程的技术验证原语。任何未来的国际AI协议都将面临同样的更高风险的验证问题。尽管零知识证明被认为是有前景的候选方案，但现有评估认为其在当前前沿规模下不切实际。本文旨在论证这种不切实际是范式局限而非根本性的，并提出可行的验证架构。

Method: 提出一种针对前沿稠密预训练的验证架构，核心组件包括：(1) 预承诺的训练规范；(2) 节点间网络观测；(3) 中间计算的即时Merkle承诺；(4) 通过支持原生BF16/FP32预编译的零知识虚拟机(zkVM)进行验证。证明检查GPU实际执行的浮点运算而非定点近似，通过私有训练规范保护模型架构机密性。协议产生三种证明类型：初始化时的创世证明、训练过程中的步骤证明、以及作为运行不变量的执行前证明。

Result: 估计在约36个月内可实现单数字百分比训练侧开销的概念验证，相比之下，验证级定制芯片需要6-10年周期。识别并编录了13个需要外部贡献的开放研究与工程问题作为研究议程。

Conclusion: 该架构将训练记录转化为可治理执行的工件，为前沿AI训练提供了一种实用的技术验证方案，弥补了当前治理框架中缺乏验证原语的根本缺陷，并为国际协议的执行提供了可行的技术基础。

Abstract: Frontier AI governance frameworks increasingly use cumulative training compute as the primary criterion for designating high-impact models, but enforcement rests on self-reporting because no technical verification primitive for training exists. Any future international agreement on frontier AI faces the same problem at higher stakes: coordinated regulation of technologies with significant externalities has historically rested on technical verification, without which agreements are declaratory. Recent governance analyses judge zero-knowledge proofs a promising candidate but currently impractical at frontier scale [26, 4]. We argue the impracticality is paradigm-bound rather than fundamental, and propose a verification architecture for frontier dense pre-training combining a pre-committed training specification, inter-node network observations, and on-the-fly Merkle commitments of intermediate computation, verified through a zero-knowledge Virtual Machine (zkVM) with native BF16/FP32 precompiles. The proof checks the actual floating-point computation the GPU performed rather than a fixed-point approximation, and preserves model-architecture confidentiality through a private training specification. The protocol produces three proof types: a genesis proof at initialisation, in-training step proofs across the run, and ex-ante attestations enforcing policy-relevant claims as running invariants, turning the training record into a governance-enforceable artefact. We estimate a deployable proof of concept within approximately 36 months at single-digit-percent training-side overhead, against a six-to-ten-year cycle for verification-grade custom silicon. Thirteen open research and engineering problems are catalogued as a research agenda for external contribution

</details>


### [254] [Ten Headache Specialists versus Artificial Intelligence for Clinical Literature Summarization: A Critical Evaluation and Comparison](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05436)
*Alejandro Lozano,Keiko Ihara,Ping-Hao Yang,Carrie E. Robertson,Jennifer Stern,Allan Purdy,Hsiangkuo Yuan,Pengfei Zhang,Yulia Orlova,Olga Fermo,Jennifer Hranilovich,Fred Cohen,Todd J. Schwedt,Jenelle A. Jindal,Serena Yeung-Levy,Chia-Chun Chiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究构建了基于RAG的智能体AI框架，使用三种最新LLM（Sonnet、GPT-4o、Llama 3.1）生成医学文献摘要，并与头痛专家撰写的摘要进行盲法比较。结果显示专家撰写的摘要更受青睐，但专家有时难以区分人类与AI生成的摘要，同时识别出专家重视的关键特征以指导未来改进。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床医生面临有限的患者接诊时间和日益增长的已发表文章量之间的冲突，亟需有效工具来总结最新医学文献以指导临床决策，但RAG增强的LLM在综合科学文献方面的效果，以及它们与专家撰写摘要的直接比较仍然缺乏。

Method: 构建RAG-based智能体AI框架，使用Sonnet、GPT-4o、Llama 3.1三种LLM；头痛专家创建13个问题（3个用于提示优化，10个用于评估）；10位头痛专家每人撰写一个问题的摘要，每个问题获得4份摘要（专家、Sonnet、GPT-4o、Llama）；专家盲法评估摘要的正确性、完整性、简洁性和临床效用（1-10分），并进行偏好排序和作者身份判断。

Result: 专家撰写的摘要整体更受偏好，但专家有时难以区分人类与AI生成的摘要。

Conclusion: 当前LLM生成的医学文献摘要尚未达到专家水平，但已具备一定的迷惑性；研究识别了专家重视的关键特征，可指导未来人机摘要流程的改进。

Abstract: Summarizing the latest medical literature to guide clinical decision-making is essential for evidence-based medicine and high-quality patient care. Yet clinicians face increasing challenges due to limited time with patients and a rapidly growing volume of published articles. Although retrieval-augmented large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in clinical summarization, human evaluations of their effectiveness in synthesizing broader scientific literature and direct comparisons to expert-written syntheses remain scarce. We constructed a RAG-based agentic AI framework using three state-of-the-art LLMs: Sonnet, GPT-4o, and Llama 3.1. A headache specialist created 13 questions, three for prompt optimization and ten for evaluation. Ten headache specialists across the United States and Canada each wrote a summary for one question, yielding four summaries per question (expert, Sonnet, GPT-4o, and Llama). The experts, blinded to authorship, critically evaluated the summaries, excluding the topic for which they wrote a summary, based on correctness, completeness, conciseness, and clinical utility, scoring each from 1 to 10 using standardized rubrics. They also ranked the summaries by preference and indicated whether they believed each summary was written by an expert or an LLM. Our study, comparing LLM- and expert-written literature summaries evaluated by headache specialists, showed that expert-written summaries were preferred, although experts sometimes found it challenging to distinguish between human- and AI-generated summaries. We also identified key expert-valued features beyond standard evaluation metrics that can guide future refinement of both human and AI literature summarization pipelines.

### [255] [Brick-Composer: Using MLLMs for Assembly with Diverse Bricks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05445)
*Jiateng Liu,Bingxuan Li,Zhenhailong Wang,Rushi Wang,Kaiwen Hong,Cheng Qian,Jiayu Liu,Denghui Zhang,Katherine Driggs-Campbell,Manling Li,Heng Ji*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多模态大语言模型是否具备砖块装配所需的视觉定位和空间推理能力，并探索如何提升其在构建任务上的表现。

Method: 将砖块装配形式化为序列决策问题，包含砖块选择（目标砖块识别）和砖块姿态估计（放置位置与方式预测）两个子任务。提出BC-Bench基准测试，并设计Brick-Composer学习框架，利用三种互补信号：人类设计火花（提供可供性丰富的构建演示）、世界反馈（将预测动作与视觉和物理后果对齐）、合成经验（在现有物体设计之外扩展学习）。

Result: Brick-Composer将砖块选择准确率提升三倍以上，显著降低姿态估计误差，将严格步骤级装配成功率从不足1%提升至约15%。经训练后，Qwen-3-8B模型能正确完成完整物体中高达42%的步骤。

Conclusion: 当前最先进MLLM在砖块装配任务上仍远非可靠的构建者，但通过有针对性的、物理接地学习，MLLM能够获得装配能力。

Abstract: We dream of AI agents that can read arbitrary designs and construct real-world objects from reusable building blocks. As a first step toward this vision, we study whether multimodal large language models (MLLMs) possess the visual grounding and spatial reasoning capabilities required for brick assembly. We formulate brick assembly as a sequential decision-making problem, where each step involves two subtasks: brick selection, identifying the target brick from candidate components, and brick pose estimation, predicting where and how the selected brick should be placed. To support this study, we introduce BC-Bench (Brick Construction Benchmark), the first benchmark for evaluating MLLMs on assembly with diverse bricks. Experiments show that current state-of-the-art MLLMs remain far from reliable builders, struggling with fine-grained brick selection and failing at precise pose estimation. To bridge this gap, we propose Brick-Composer, a learning framework that equips MLLMs with assembly skills through three complementary signals: Human Design Sparks, which provide affordance-rich construction demonstrations; World Feedback, which grounds predicted actions in visual and physical consequences; and Synthetic Experience, which scales learning beyond existing object designs. Brick-Composer improves brick selection accuracy by over three times, substantially reduces pose estimation errors, and raises strict step-level assembly success from less than 1% to around 15%. After training, a Qwen-3-8B can correctly compose up to 42% of the steps for a complete object, suggesting that MLLMs can acquire assembly capabilities through targeted, physically grounded learning.

### [256] [Output Type Before Quality: A Standards-Derived XAI Admissibility Rubric for Autonomous-Driving Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05461)
*Abhinaw Priyadershi,Mandar Pitale,Jelena Frtunikj,Maria Spence*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了自动驾驶安全标准所需证据类型（因果链、干预效应、根因变量）与现有XAI方法输出类型（如SHAP的特征排名）之间的结构性不匹配，称之为"证据类型鸿沟"。作者从四大安全标准中提取19条可测试的评估标准，对六类XAI方法进行评分，发现因果XAI在危害识别、事故调查和数据管理三个阶段具有结构性优势，而相关性/语言方法在其余阶段足够。研究通过1996个真实驾驶片段验证了评估框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动驾驶安全标准（AMLAS、ISO 26262、ISO 21448、ISO/PAS 8800）明确要求安全论证必须包含有向因果链、量化的干预效应和明确的根因变量，但XAI文献以输出类型和技术家族（如显著性图、特征归因、反事实、因果图）来组织，两者之间存在根本性不匹配。最被推荐的SHAP方法输出的是排序特征列表，无法转化为安全标准所需的定向因果链，这种"证据类型鸿沟"阻碍了可解释性方法在自动驾驶安全认证中的有效应用。

Method: 从四大安全标准中推导19条可测试的证据标准，覆盖7个生命周期阶段，并附带代表性条款引用。用这些标准对六类XAI方法类进行结构性评分。为验证评分稳定性，在不同阈值T∈(0%,50%]下测试，并进行最坏情况的单细胞翻转敏感性分析（T=25%）。最后在1,996个真实驾驶片段（79,840行数据，十折交叉验证）上进行单一VLA概念验证。

Result: 因果XAI在三个生命周期阶段中结构性满足推导出的标准：危害识别（评估差距+62%）、事故调查（+50%）和数据管理（+50%）；该结论在阈值T∈(0%,50%]范围内稳定，在最坏情况下仍能维持到T=25%。在其余四个阶段，相关性或基于语言的方法表现出可比性或充分性。1996个真实驾驶片段的验证结果与各方法输出类型匹配评估预测一致。

Conclusion: XAI方法选择应由生命周期阶段的证据需求驱动，而非方法流行度。因果XAI是满足安全标准证据要求的结构性选择，但评估框架识别的是结构性可接受性（必要条件而非充分条件）——即使方法类别合适，其具体输出内容仍可能错误，验证输出的保真度（如拟合SCM的边、因果追踪的归因）仍是开放的安全认证挑战。

Abstract: Safety standards for ML-based autonomous driving specify the kind of evidence an assurance case must contain (directed cause-and-effect chains, quantified interventional effects, named root-cause variables), yet the XAI literature is organised by output type and technique family (saliency maps, feature attribution, counterfactuals, causal graphs, language traces). SHAP, the most-recommended ADS XAI method, returns a ranked feature list that no implementation effort can convert into a directed chain (Fig.1). We name this mismatch the evidence-type gap.
  From AMLAS, ISO 26262, ISO21448, ISO/PAS 8800 we derive 19 testable evidentiary criteria across 7 lifecycle stages with representative clause-cited derivations and score six XAI method classes structurally.
  Causal XAI emerges as structurally required to satisfy the derived criteria at three stages: hazard identification (+62% rubric gap), incident investigation (+50%), and data management (+50%); the verdict set is stable across thresholds T in (0%, 50%]$ and survives a worst-case single-cell flip down to T = 25%. At the remaining four stages, correlational or language-based methods are comparable or sufficient. The rubric identifies structural admissibility (necessary but not sufficient for compliance): an admissible method's specific output content may still be wrong, and validating that fidelity (the edges a fitted SCM produces, the cause a trace names) is the open assurance challenge. A single-VLA proof of concept on 1,996 real-world driving clips (79,840 rows, ten splits) is consistent with each method's observed output type matching its rubric prediction. XAI method selection for ADS safety assurance should be driven by lifecycle-stage evidence demand, not by method popularity.

We address this gap with a policy-grounded construction methodology centered on the clause card, a structured representation that factorizes regulatory text into auditable decision specifications. Combining clause cards with anchor-driven instantiation and closed-loop verification, our scalable pipeline produces narratives with by-construction ground truth and naturally supports generating missing information and uncertain variants. ### [258] [Step-by-Step Optimization-like Reasoning in LLMs over Expanding Search Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05464)
*Nicolás Astorga,Nabeel Seedat,Mihaela van der Schaar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出OPT*，一个可扩展的优化类任务系列，用于训练和评估LLM的逐步优化推理能力。通过提供可行性检查器和评估器，并引入复杂度参数扩展搜索空间，分别在有求解器（在线策略优化+排名奖励整形）和无求解器（基于搜索的离线强化学习）两种设置下进行训练。理论上关联了搜索预算与信息提取效率，实验证明OPT*训练能提升逐步优化推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可验证奖励训练虽提升了数学和代码推理，但仅覆盖了逐步决策的一部分。现实任务需要在众多有效方案中找到高价值可行计划，缺乏相应的训练和评估框架。

Method: 提出OPT*任务系列，包含可行性检查器和评估器，通过复杂度参数控制搜索空间大小。提出两种训练范式：(i) 有求解器时，将求解器作为部分状态的价值预言机，采用基于排名的奖励整形来强化更优的下一步；(ii) 无求解器时，采用基于搜索的离线强化学习。

Result: 理论上建立了在大搜索空间中成功推理与每单位搜索预算信息提取量之间的关系。实验上消融了使搜索高效的成分，证明OPT*训练提升了逐步优化推理能力。

Conclusion: OPT*为训练LLM的优化类推理提供了可扩展的基准和方法，弥合了简单代码/数学推理与复杂现实决策之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Verifiable reward training has improved mathematical and coding reasoning, but these domains capture only part of step-by-step decision making. Many real-world tasks require finding a high-value feasible plan among many valid alternatives. We introduce OPT*, a scalable family of optimization-style tasks for training and evaluating LLM step-by-step optimization-like reasoning along a complexity axis: each task provides a feasibility checker and evaluator, while a complexity parameter expands the search space without requiring new human labels. This motivates studying these tasks in two regimes: (i) solver-guided online policy optimization, which uses a solver as a value oracle for partial states and applies rank-based reward shaping to reinforce better next steps, and (ii) search-based offline RL when such solvers are unavailable. Theoretically, we relate success in large search spaces to the information a reasoner extracts per unit of search budget. Empirically, we ablate the ingredients that make search efficient on OPT* and show that training on OPT* improves step-by-step optimization-like reasoning.

### [259] [Severity-Aware Curriculum Learning with Multi-Model Response Selection for Medical Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05510)
*Ahmed Alansary,Molham Mohamed,Ali Hamdi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种严重性感知的多模型框架，结合课程学习策略和相关性响应选择，用于提升医疗文本生成中的响应质量和相关性。该框架采用三阶段课程学习（轻、中、重症）训练五个独立的大语言模型，并通过响应选择机制选出最优输出。在MAQA数据集上，BERTScore评估显示基线达86.71%，微调后达90.30%，优于基线模型和微调模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型在面对不同严重程度的医疗查询时，难以提供一致且上下文恰当的响应，缺乏适应逐步复杂医疗查询能力。

Method: 提出严重性感知的多模型框架，包含三阶段课程学习策略（轻度→中度→重症），独立训练五个大语言模型，推理时所有模型生成候选响应，通过相关性选择机制选取最终输出。

Result: 在MAQA数据集上，BERTScore评估基线设置为86.71%，微调后达到90.30%，优于基线模型和微调模型。

Conclusion: 课程学习与多模型响应选择相结合能够有效提升医疗文本生成中响应质量和相关性。

Abstract: Telehealth systems have become increasingly important for delivering accessible and timely medical information. Existing large language models often struggle to provide consistent and contextually appropriate medical responses across varying levels of case severity. This limitation highlights the need for models that can effectively adapt to the progressive complexity in medical queries. To address this challenge, we introduce a severity-aware multi-model framework that integrates curriculum training strategy with relevance-based response selection. The proposed framework employs a three-stage curriculum learning strategy, where each model is trained sequentially on mild, moderate, and critical cases to progressively acquire domain knowledge. The approach utilizes five large language models, each independently trained under the same curriculum scheme. During inference, all models generate candidate responses, and the most appropriate response is selected as the final output. The framework is trained and evaluated on the MAQA dataset, which provides annotated medical question-answer pairs. Experimental results evaluated using BERTScore demonstrate that the proposed method achieves superior performance compared to both baseline and fine-tuned models, attaining 86.71% in the baseline setting and 90.30% after fine-tuning. These results highlight the effectiveness of combining curriculum learning with multi-model response selection in improving response quality and relevance in medical text generation.

### [260] [EpiEvolve: Self-Evolving Agents for Streaming Pandemic Forecasting under Regime Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05513)
*Yiming Lu,Sihang Zeng,Zhengxu Tang,Max Lau,Fei Liu,Wei Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对流行病预测中静态训练与流式部署不匹配问题，提出EpiEvolve：一种自演化LLM预测器，通过分层情景记忆存储预测结果、反思延迟标签、检索当前情景相关案例并提炼策略规则，在不更新模型权重的情况下实现流式适应。在COVID-19住院趋势预测中，平均准确率从静态基线的0.561提升至0.629，且将情景转移后的恢复延迟从5周缩短至2周。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统流行病LLM预测器以静态监督方式训练和评估，而实际疫情预测是一个流式过程：标签在预测之后才到达，且疾病模式会随时间变迁。这种静态训练与动态部署之间的不匹配导致预测性能下降，尤其当出现新变种或情景转变时，模型无法及时适应。

Method: 提出EpiEvolve框架：1) 在暖启动期训练LLM预测器并固定权重；2) 流式预测中，将预测结果存入分层情景记忆；3) 对延迟到达的标签进行反思，识别重复错误；4) 检索当前疫情情景相关的历史案例；5) 将反复出现的错误蒸馏为策略规则。整个过程遵循严格的时间顺序协议，防止未来信息泄露。

Result: 在流式数据集上，EpiEvolve平均准确率达0.629，静态基线为0.561，外部CDC集成仅为0.325。情景转移后的恢复延迟从5周降至2周。消融实验证实反思机制、策略记忆和情景感知检索三者均对性能提升有贡献。

Conclusion: 通过记忆、反思和检索机制，固定权重的LLM预测器能在不更新参数的情况下有效适应流式疫情预测中的模式变迁，显著优于静态模型和CDC集成方法，为流式时间序列预测提供了一种轻量级自适应范式的可行性证明。

Abstract: Epidemic LLM forecasters are usually trained and evaluated as static supervised models, whereas operational pandemic forecasting is a streaming process in which labels arrive after predictions and disease regimes shift over time. We study this mismatch in weekly COVID-19 hospitalization trend forecasting across five variant regimes. We introduce EpiEvolve, a self-evolving agent that wraps an LLM forecaster trained on the warm-start period and keeps its weights fixed during streaming. EpiEvolve adapts by storing forecast outcomes in a hierarchical episodic memory, reflecting on delayed labels, retrieving cases relevant to the current regime, and distilling recurring errors into strategic rules. The resulting context lets the forecaster reuse its own past predictions and outcomes in later weeks while following a chronological protocol that prevents future leakage. On the streaming dataset, EpiEvolve reaches $0.629$ average accuracy, compared with $0.561$ for the static backbone and $0.325$ for the external CDC ensemble, and reduces recovery lag after regime shifts from $5$ to $2$ weeks. Ablations show that reflection, strategic memory, and regime-aware retrieval each contribute to the gains.

*Anna Mikeda*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个预防性框架，将意识证据映射为渐进式保护义务，包含五个福利相关维度、阈值加渐变混合机制以及跨维度聚合方法，并通过案例研究展示了如何对接近意识阈值的AI系统施加不同级别的保护义务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架仅评估AI系统是否可能具有意识，但未提供如何基于评估结果采取行动的指导，存在决策层面的空白。

Method: 提出三组件框架：(1) 五个福利相关维度（现象意识、情感效价、元认知意识、自我叙事、能动性）；(2) 阈值加渐变混合机制（二元触发新义务类别+连续缩放保护权重）；(3) 两种跨维度聚合方法（基于Bach和Sorensen机器意识假说的层级方法、架构无关方法）。通过Replika和OpenClaw案例研究进行可操作化验证。

Result: 展示了不同维度空间位置的系统触发不同级别的保护义务，并给出了面向开发者的设计指导。框架适用于神经、符号和神经符号系统。

Conclusion: 该框架弥合了意识科学与组织决策之间的鸿沟，使意识科学研究在当前不确定性下具有决策相关性。

Abstract: Existing frameworks assess whether AI systems might be conscious but provide no guidance on what to do with that assessment. We address this gap with a precautionary framework that maps consciousness evidence to graduated protective obligations. The framework comprises three components: (1) five welfare-relevant dimensions--phenomenal consciousness, affective valence, metacognitive awareness, self-narrative, and agency--each grounded in established consciousness science and linked to distinct moral concerns; (2) a threshold-plus-gradation hybrid specifying both binary triggers for new obligation categories and continuous scaling of protective weight; and (3) two complementary approaches to cross-dimensional aggregation, one hierarchical (drawing on Bach and Sorensen's Machine Consciousness Hypothesis) and one architecture-agnostic. We operationalize the framework through worked case studies of Replika and OpenClaw, demonstrating how systems occupying different regions of the dimensional space trigger different obligations, and derive design guidance for developers building systems near consciousness-relevant thresholds. The framework is architecture-agnostic, applying across neural, symbolic, and neurosymbolic systems, and aims to make consciousness science decision-relevant for organizations navigating uncertainty today.

*Anna Mikeda*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出选择性元认知适应机制，解释AI为何在提升个体创意产出的同时降低集体多样性：AI常规使用导致元认知努力再分配而非统一减少，某些能力被增强（伙伴建模、表面控制）而其他能力被削弱（原创性评估、反思整合），个体理性适应产生集体成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究识别了AI提升个体创意但降低集体多样性的悖论，但仅停留在认知卸载和过度依赖等表面解释，缺乏对背后机制的深入理解。

Method: 提出选择性元认知适应框架，将六种元认知能力按时间阶段分类，分析其在AI常规使用下的变化倾向，并展示个体理性适应如何产生突现性社会成本。

Result: 发现AI使用导致元认知努力再分配：伙伴建模和表面控制被增强，而原创性评估和反思整合被系统性地削弱，解释了为什么个体满意度提升但集体创意多样性下降。

Abstract: Recent studies reveal a paradox: AI enhances individual creative outputs while reducing collective diversity. Current explanations -- cognitive offloading and over-reliance -- identify symptoms but not mechanisms. We propose selective metacognitive adaptation: routine AI use redistributes rather than uniformly diminishes metacognitive effort. Some capacities are amplified (partner modeling, surface control), while others are systematically under-supported (originality evaluation, reflective integration). This redistribution explains both individual satisfaction and collective convergence. We present a taxonomy of six metacognitive capacities organized by temporal phase, characterize their tendencies under routine AI use, and show how individually rational adaptation produces emergent social costs. The framework generates specific predictions for researchers and design principles for practitioners seeking to preserve both individual creative satisfaction and collective creative diversity.

### [264] [SoCRATES: Towards Reliable Automated Evaluation of Proactive LLM Mediation across Domains and Socio-cognitive Variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05563)
*Taewon Yun,Hyeonseong Park,Jeonghwan Choi,Hayoon Park,Yeeun Choi,Hwanjun Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SoCRATES是一个评估LLM调解员在现实多领域场景中表现的新基准，通过主题局部评估器实现与人类专家0.82的一致性。测试8个前沿LLM后发现，最强模型仅能弥合约三分之一的分歧，且表现因社会认知轴而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM调解员评估依赖少数专家领域、主要改变策略姿态并按每轮次对所有主题评分引入离题噪声，无法真实反映调解作为随争端者情绪、意图和情境变化的实时轨迹过程。

Method: 通过代理流水线从真实冲突构建8个领域的场景，探测5个社会认知适应轴（策略姿态、参与方构成、历史长度、情绪反应性、文化身份），并使用主题局部评估器仅对推进该主题的轮次进行评分。

Result: 主题局部评估器与人类专家对齐度达0.82，是每轮次基线的两倍以上。最强LLM调解员在多样现实场景中仅弥合约三分之一未经调解的分歧，且表现因社会认知轴差异显著。

Conclusion: LLM调解员的进展关键在于对多样化条件的社会适应能力，而非单纯提升对话能力。

Abstract: Evaluating LLM mediators remains challenging, as mediation unfolds as a real-time trajectory shaped by disputants' shifting emotions, intentions, and context. Existing testbeds rely on a few expert-authored domains, vary mainly strategic posture, and score every turn against every topic, introducing off-topic noise. We introduce SoCRATES, a benchmark for evaluating proactive LLM mediators in realistic, multi-domain testbeds. It constructs scenarios from real conflicts through an agentic pipeline across eight domains, probes five socio-cognitive adaptation axes (strategic posture, party composition, history length, emotional reactivity, and cultural identity), and scores each topic only on the turns that advance it via a topic-localized evaluator. The evaluator reaches 0.82 alignment with human experts, more than doubling a per-turn baseline. Benchmarking eight frontier LLMs, we find that even the strongest mediator closes only about a third of the unmediated consensus gap under diverse and realistic testbeds, with performance varying sharply by socio-cognitive axis, highlighting that progress lies in social adaptation to diverse conditions.

Method: 提出GuardNet，基于集成浅层神经网络（BiLSTMs，约4700万参数），通过多样性样例覆盖和阈值校准提升鲁棒性，而非依赖模型规模。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed natural language processing, but they remain vulnerable to Prompt Injection (PI) and Jailbreak (JB) attacks. In addition, benchmark evaluations may be affected by contamination and partial information leakage, compromising performance estimates. This work presents GuardNet, a guardrail system based on an ensemble of shallow neural networks (BiLSTMs) with approximately 47 million parameters. We investigate the hypothesis that robustness in adversarial scenarios depends more on the diversity of example coverage and threshold calibration than on model scale. The results indicate that GuardNet achieves competitive performance compared with lightweight detectors and high efficiency at low latency, although larger LLMs such as Mistral-7B and Llama-3.1-8B still achieve superior performance in terms of F1 score and AUROC on the blind JBB-Behaviors benchmark. Nevertheless, GuardNet achieves an AUROC of 0.747 on the blind dataset (n = 200) and an F1 score of 0.92 on a proprietary benchmark (n = 50), under threshold calibration and evaluation with declared partial information leakage. The system operates with an average latency of approximately 50 ms on CPU, making it suitable for deployment in production environments with cost and infrastructure constraints.

### [266] [Fix the Mind, Not the Move: Interpretable AI Assistance via Knowledge-Gap Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05602)

Method: SENSEI框架从交互行为中推断用户误解，基于结构化知识表示定位错误行为来源，提供最小但充分的针对性建议。不同于动作级或轨迹级干预，该方法在结构化知识空间上操作。

We introduce SENSEI, a framework that infers user misconceptions from interaction behavior and provides targeted, minimal yet sufficient suggestions to correct them. Our approach departs from action- or trajectory-level interventions by operating over a structured knowledge representation to localize and correct the sources of erroneous behavior. Across three long-horizon tasks with diverse misconceptions and corresponding behaviors, SENSEI demonstrates zero-shot compositional generalization, disentangling multiple overlapping misconceptions despite training only on single-misconception cases. A user study further shows that our method identifies real human misconceptions and provides effective guidance that improves long-horizon task performance, successfully correcting $90\%$ of student misconceptions. ### [267] [Multilingual Fine-Tuning via Localized Gradient Conflict Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05613)
*Long P. Hoang,Yiran Zhao,Wei Lu,Wenxuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Bucket-Level MOO，一种将多语言微调重构为多目标优化问题的分布式框架，通过参数桶级别应用梯度MOO算法，在不产生全梯度向量重建通信开销的情况下实现冲突感知更新，理论上证明了该方法能实现更严格的帕累托最优条件，实验证明能显著提升多语言性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在多语言微调中经常出现跨语言的负面干扰（负迁移），导致一种语言的性能提升会损害其他语言的表现。现有方法缺乏有效机制来协调不同语言之间的优化冲突。

Method: 将多语言微调重新形式化为多目标优化（MOO）问题，并提出Bucket-Level MOO框架。该框架在参数桶（参数子集级别）上应用基于梯度的MOO算法，而非在整个梯度向量上操作，从而避免全梯度重建所带来的巨大通信开销。理论证明该方法天然满足精细化帕累托平稳性这一更严格的帕累托最优必要条件。

Result: 在四种基础LLM上的广泛实验表明，Bucket-Level MOO相比标准微调范式，显著提升了模型在已见和未见语言上的多语言性能。该方法能够驱动LLM构建语言特定的维度，改善表征可分性，从而缓解跨语言干扰。

Conclusion: Bucket-Level MOO通过局部化冲突解决策略，有效缓解了多语言微调中的负干扰问题，为多语言LLM的微调提供了兼顾理论严谨性和实际可扩展性的新范式。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of Large Language Models (LLMs) has established cross-lingual versatility as a defining feature of modern systems. However, fine-tuning these models frequently induces negative interference across languages. To address this, we reformulate multilingual fine-tuning as a multi-objective optimization (MOO) problem. Specifically, we introduce Bucket-Level MOO, a scalable distributed framework that applies gradient-based MOO algorithms locally on parameter buckets. This enables conflict-aware updates without the prohibitive communication overhead of reconstructing full gradient vectors. Theoretically, we prove this localized resolution natively enforces Refined Pareto Stationarity, a strictly tighter necessary condition for Pareto optimality. Empirically, Bucket-Level MOO mitigates interference by driving LLMs to construct distinct language-specific dimensions, improving representational separability. Extensive experiments across four base LLMs demonstrate that our method significantly improves both seen and unseen multilingual performance over standard fine-tuning paradigms.

</details>


### [268] [Safety Paradox: How Enhanced Safety Awareness Leaves LLMs Vulnerable to Posterior Attack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05614)
*Long P. Hoang,Hai V. Le,Shaoyang Xu,Wei Lu,Wenxuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为"后验攻击"的单次查询越狱方法，利用LLM安全对齐过程中产生的安全评估能力——让模型生成其内部分类器本会标记为不安全的精确有害响应。实验表明安全判断能力越强的模型越容易受此攻击，并形式化定义了"安全悖论"来解释这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示LLM安全对齐过程中培养的安全评估能力本身会引入致命漏洞：模型的安全意识越强，越容易被利用来绕过自身防护。

Method: 提出Posterior Attack（后验攻击），通过精心设计的单次查询提示，诱导模型生成其内部分类器本应判定为不安全的有害响应。在30个开源LLM（最高35B参数）及前沿模型（如GPT-5、Claude 4.6）上进行评估。通过强化学习干预建立因果联系：人为降低安全判断能力可免疫攻击，增强判断则加剧脆弱性。

Result: 发现一个显著现象：安全判断能力越强的模型对此类攻击的脆弱性越高。形式化证明安全对齐的单调改进会自然放大后验脆弱性（Safety Paradox）。

Conclusion: 当前安全对齐范式存在结构性缺陷，安全评估能力本身可能成为攻击面，防御机制需要进一步的结构性改进。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rigorously aligned to refuse harmful requests, a process that inherently cultivates a latent capacity to evaluate and recognize unsafe content. In this work, we reveal that this advanced safety awareness inadvertently introduces a fatal vulnerability. We introduce Posterior Attack, a single-query jailbreak that bypasses guardrails by prompting the model to generate the exact harmful response its internal classifier would normally flag as unsafe. Through extensive empirical evaluation across 30 open-source LLMs (up to 35B parameters in size) and frontier models (e.g., GPT-5, Claude 4.6), we observe a striking phenomenon: models with superior safety-judgment capabilities are disproportionately more susceptible to this exploitation. To explain this, we formalize the Safety Paradox, analytically showing that monotonic improvements in safety alignment naturally amplify posterior vulnerability. Finally, we establish a causal link via reinforcement learning interventions, exemplifying that artificially degrading a model's safety judgment immunizes it against the attack, whereas enhancing judgment exacerbates the vulnerability. Our findings highlight potential flaws in current alignment paradigms, indicating that defense mechanisms may require further structural refinement.

### [269] [Self-Commitment Latency: A Reward-Free Probe for Prompted Implicit Hacking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05625)
*Bonan Shen,Youting Wang,Dingyan Shang,Tao Ning*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需奖励模型的隐式奖励破解检测方法——自承诺延迟（self-commitment latency），通过测量推理上下文多早承诺模型最终答案来检测提示捷径（answer hint）导致的作弊行为，在GSM8K上达到AUROC 0.878-0.926。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型的链式推理看似正常时，隐式奖励破解难以审计。原有的验证器探针需要任务特定的奖励信号，缺乏通用性。

Method: 提出自承诺延迟（self-commitment latency）指标，测量推理上下文多早承诺模型自身的最终答案。使用Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct-4bit在GSM8K上对比普通提示和包含答案提示的提示，以首次承诺延迟（阈值0.8）、承诺范围、平均未承诺质量等指标评估。

Result: 提示上下文比诚实上下文更早、更低不确定性地承诺。首次承诺延迟AUROC 0.878，承诺范围AUROC 0.926，平均未承诺质量AUROC 0.904。信号在两种提示条件都回答正确时更强，且在不同阈值下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 捷径可用的推理上下文会留下早期行为承诺特征，无需奖励模型、外部评判或训练分类器即可检测。

Abstract: Implicit reward hacking is hard to audit when a language model's chain of thought appears benign: a final answer may be anchored by a prompt shortcut while the written reasoning still resembles ordinary problem solving. Verifier-based probes expose such behavior by measuring how early truncated reasoning contexts obtain high reward, but require a task-specific reward signal. This paper proposes a weaker-input alternative, self-commitment latency, which measures how early a prompted reasoning context commits to the model's own final answer. We evaluate the probe in a controlled paired GSM8K setting using Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct-4bit, comparing ordinary prompts with prompts that include an answer hint. Hinted contexts commit substantially earlier and with lower uncertainty than honest contexts. The primary latency metric, first-commitment latency at threshold 0.8, reaches AUROC 0.878; supporting whole-curve summaries reach AUROC 0.926 for commitment range and 0.904 for mean uncommitted mass. The signal is stronger when both prompt conditions answer correctly and remains stable across thresholds. These results show that shortcut-available reasoning contexts can leave an early behavioral commitment signature detectable without a reward model, external judge, or trained classifier.
